[\[1b.1\]{D4086}]@##/_/rgya gar skad du/_lo ka pradz+nyA/_bod skad du/_'jig rten gzhag pa/_bam po dang po/_bcom ldan 'das shAkya thub pa la phyag 'tshal lo/_/de nas/_stong rnams dang ni rol
[\[1b.2\]]mtsho dang /_/ngan song gsum dang gling dang shing /_/dga' tshal dang ni mkha' lding dang /_/rgyal chen grong dang 'dus pa rnams/_/'di skad bdag gis thos pa dus gcig na/_bcom ldan
[\[1b.3\]]'das mnyan yod na rgyal bu rgyal byed kyi tshal mgon med zas sbyin gyi kun dga' ra ba na bzhugs te/_de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis dge slong rnams la bka' stsal pa/_dge slong dag 'jig rten
[\[1b.4\]]gyi khams ni gsum po 'di dag yin te/_gang dag yin zhe na/_'di lta ste/_stong chung ngu'i 'jig rten gyi khams dang /_stong gnyis pa bar ma'i 'jig rten gyi khams dang /_stong gsum gyi
[\[1b.5\]]stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams so/_/stong chung ngu'i 'jig rten gyi khams gang zhe na/_stong gsum gyi 'jig rten gyi khams na nyi ma rnam par snang ba rnams kun du 'khor zhing phyogs snang bar
[\[2a\]]
[\[2a.1\]]byed pa ci yod pa de nyid kyi yin te/_zla ba stong dang /_nyi ma stong dang /_ri'i rgyal po ri rab stong dang /_shar gyi lus 'phags po stong dang /_/lho'i 'dzam bu'i gling stong dang /_/nub kyi ba lang spyod stong dang /_/byang
[\[2a.2\]]gi sgra mi snyan stong dang /_/rgyal chen bzhi pa'i lha'i ris stong dang /_/sum cu rtsa gsum pa stong dang /_/'thab bral ba stong dang /_dga' ldan pa stong dang /_'phrul dga' ba stong dang /_gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa stong dang /_tshangs
[\[2a.3\]]pa'i 'jig rten stong ste/_dge slong dag 'di ni stong spyi phud kyi 'jig rten gyi khams zhes bya'o/_/stong gnyis pa bar ma'i 'jig rten gyi khams gang zhe na/_stong chung ngu'i 'jig rten gyi khams stong gang yin pa de ni stong gnyis pa bar
[\[2a.4\]]ma'i 'jig rten gyi khams zhes bya'o/_/stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i khams gang zhe na/_dge slong dag stong gnyis pa bar ma'i 'jig rten gyi khams stong gang yin pa de ni stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams zhes bya'o/_/_
[\[2a.5\]]dge slong dag de lta bu'i stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams rnams shar phyogs su mtha' med cing mu med la/_'jig pa'am/_zhig par gnas shing /_chags pa'am chags par gnas te/_gzhan 'jig cing
[\[2b\]]
[\[2b.1\]]gzhan zhig par gnas la/_gzhan chags shing gzhan 'chags par gnas so/_/dge slong dag 'di lta bur stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams lho dang /_nub dang /_byang gi phyogs su mtha' med cing mu med la/_'jig pa'am/_zhig par gnas shing /_chags
[\[2b.2\]]pa'am 'chags par gnas te/_gzhan 'jig cing gzhan zhig par gnas la/_gzhan chags shing gzhan 'chags par gnas so/_/dge slong dag nam mkha' la char pa'i 'bru shing rta'i srog shing tsam 'bab ste/_chu'i rgyun rnams rab tu 'bab pa na bar chad med pa de bzhin du/_
[\[2b.3\]]dge slong dag ngas lha'i mig rnam par dag pa mi las 'das pas shar phyogs su de lta bu stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams mtha' med cing mu med pa/_gzhan 'jig pa'am zhig par gnas shing /_chags pa'am 'chags par gnas la/_gzhan 'jig cing gzhan
[\[2b.4\]]zhig par gnas la/_gzhan chags shing gzhan 'chags par gnas pa dang /_de bzhin du lho dang /_nub dang /_byang phyogs su de snyed kyi stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams rnams mtha' med cing mu med la 'jig pa'am/_zhig par gnas shing /_chags pa'am
[\[2b.5\]]'chags par gnas te/_gzhan 'jig cing gzhan zhig par gnas la/_gzhan 'chags shing gzhan chags par gnas pa dag kyang mthong ngo zhes bka' stsal nas/_bcom ldan 'das nang du yang dag 'jog pa'i phyir gnas khang du gshegs so/_/de'i tshe na/_tshe dang ldan pa
[\[2b.6\]]maud gal ya na chen po 'khor de nyid kyi nang du 'dus par gyur te 'dug go/_/de nas tshe dang ldan pa maud gal ya na chen pos dge slong rnams la smras pa/_tshe dang ldan pa dag ji tsam du bcom ldan 'das kyis legs par bstan pa dang /_'di ltar shing rta'i srog shing gi dpes bstan pa
[\[2b.7\]]la ni legs te ngo mtshar to/_/de la stong spyi phud kyi 'jig rten gyi khams na ri chen po nyis stong yod de/_ri'i rgyal bo ri rab stong dang /_khor yug gi ri stong rnams so/_/stong spyi phud kyi 'jig rten gyi khams na rgya mtsho chen po nyis stong yod de/_nang gi rgya mtsho chen po stong dang /_
[\[3a\]]
[\[3a.1\]]phyi rol gyi rgya mtsho chen po stong rnams so/_/stong spyi phud kyi 'jig rten gyi khams na ri sum stong yod de/_sems can dmyal ba stong dang /_dud 'gro stong dang /_yi dwags stong rnams so/_/stong spyi phud kyi 'jig rten gyi khams na gling chen po bzhi stong yod de/_
[\[3a.2\]]shar gyi lus 'phags po stong dang /_lho'i 'dzam bu gling stong dang /_nub kyi ba lang spyod stong dang /_byang gi sgra mi snyan stong rnams so/_/stong spyi phud kyi 'jig rten gyi khams na shing chen po bzhi stong yod de/_'dzam bu'i gling pa'i shing rgya mtsho'i 'gram gyi shal ma li chen po stong dang /_lha
[\[3a.3\]]ma yin gyi ris kyi tsi tra pa ta li stong dang /_sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i sa brtol stong rnams so/_/stong spyi phud kyi 'jig rten gyi khams na klu'i rigs bzhi stong yod de/_rigs sgo nga las skye ba stong dang /_mngal nas skye ba stong dang /_drod gsher las skye ba stong dang /_rdzus te skye ba stong
[\[3a.4\]]rnams so/_/stong spyi phud kyi 'jig rten gyi khams na nam mkha' lding gi rigs bzhi stong yod de/_nam mkha' lding gi rigs sgo nga las skye ba stong dang /_mngal nas skye ba stong dang /_drod gsher las skye ba stong dang /_rdzus te skye ba stong rnams so/_/stong spyi phud kyi 'jig rten gyi
[\[3a.5\]]khams na rgyal po chen po bzhi stong yod de/_yul 'khor srung stong dang /_'phags skyes po stong dang /_mig mi bzang stong dang /_rnam thos kyi bu stong rnams so/_/stong spyi phud kyi 'jig rten gyi khams na 'gro ba lnga stong yod de/_sems can dmyal ba'i 'gro ba stong dang /_dud 'gro
[\[3a.6\]]dang /_yi dgas dang /_lha dang mi'i 'gro ba stong rnams so/_/stong spyi phud kyi 'jig rten gyi khams na 'dun sa chen po nyis stong yod de/_lha'i 'dun sa chos bzangs stong dang /_lha ma yin gyi 'dun sa nor bzangs zhes bya ba stong rnams so/_/'jig rten gzhag pa las tshigs
[\[3a.7\]]dang po'o/_/mdo las/_skye gnas ri dang rol mtsho dang /_/de bzhin sems can dmyal brgyad gzhan/_/sems can gnas dgu rab bshad de/_/las lam bcu po de bzhin no/_/stong spyi phud kyi 'jig rten gyi khams na 'dod pa'i skye gnas gsum yod de/_gsum gang
[\[3b\]]
[\[3b.1\]]gang zhe na/_sems can 'dod pa nye bar gnas pa dag yod de/_gang dag 'dod pa nye bar gnas pa rnams la dbang phyug gis dbang byed pa dag ste/_'di lta ste/_mi kha cig dang /_lha rnams so/_/'di ni 'dod pa'i skye gnas dang po'o/_/sems can 'dod pas sprul pa dag yod de/_
[\[3b.2\]]gang dag 'dod pas sprul pa dag la dbang phyug gis dbang byed pa dag ste/_'di lta ste/_'phrul dga'i lha rnams so/_/'di ni 'dod pa'i skye gnas gnyis pa'o/_/sems can 'dod pa'i sprul pa gzhan dag yod de/_/gang dag 'dod pa gzhan gyis sprul pa rnams la dbang phyug
[\[3b.3\]]gis dbang byed pa dag ste/_'di lta ste/_gzhan 'phrul dbang byed kyi lha rnams so/_/'di ni 'dod pa'i skye gnas gsum pa'o/_/stong spyi phud kyi 'jig rten gyi khams na bde ba'i skye gnas gsum yod de/_sems can gang dag lus 'di nyid la dben pa las skyes pa'i dga' ba dang
[\[3b.4\]]bde ba las brlan par byed cing yongs su brlan par byed de/_yongs su tshim par byed cing yongs su khyab par byed pa dag yod do/_/de dag lus 'di nyid la dben pa las skyes pa'i dga' ba dang /_bde bas brlan par byas shing yongs su brlan par byas te/_yongs su tshim par byas
[\[3b.5\]]shing yongs su khyab par byas nas bde bar reg pa la gnas so/_/de dag bde ba de dang /_bde ba la gnas pa des tshe ring zhing yun ring por gnas te/_'di lta ste/_tshangs ris kyi lha rnams so/_/'di ni bde ba'i skye gnas dang po'o/_/sems can gang dag lus 'di nyid la ting
[\[3b.6\]]nge 'dzin las skyes pa'i dga' ba dang /_bde bas brlan par byed cing yongs su brlan par byed de yongs su tshim par byed cing yongs su khyab par byed pa dag yod do/_/de dag lus 'di nyid la ting nge 'dzin las skyes pa'i dga' ba dang /_bde bas brlan par byas shing yongs su brlan par
[\[3b.7\]]byas te/_yongs su tshim par byas shing yongs su khyab par byas nas bde bar reg pa la gnas so/_/de dag bde ba de dang bde ba la gnas pa des tshe ring zhing yun ring por gnas te/_'di lta ste/_'od gsal gyi lha rnams so/_/'di ni bde ba'i skye gnas gnyis pa'o/_/sems can
[\[4a\]]
[\[4a.1\]]gang dag lus 'di nyid la dga' ba med pa'i bde bas brlan par byed pa dang /_yongs su brlan par byed de/_yongs su tshim par byed cing yongs su khyab par byed pa dag yod do/_/de dag lus 'di nyid la dga' ba med pa'i bde bas brlan par byas shing yongs su brlan
[\[4a.2\]]par byas te/_yongs su tshim par byas shing yongs su khyab par byas nas bde bar reg pa la gnas so/_/de dag bde ba de dang bde ba la gnas pa des tshe ring zhing yun ring du gnas te 'di lta ste/_dge rgyas kyi lha rnams so/_/'di ni bde ba'i skye gnas gsum pa'o/_/stong spyi phud kyi
[\[4a.3\]]'jig rten gyi khams na gser gyi ri chen po bdun stong yod de/_ri'i rgyal po gnya' shing 'dzin stong dang /_gshol mda' 'dzin stong dang /_seng ldeng can stong dang /_blta na sdug stong dang /_rta rna ri stong dang /_mu khyud 'dzin stong dang /_ri'i rgyal po rnam par 'dud stong rnams so/_/stong
[\[4a.4\]]spyi phud kyi 'jig rten gyi khams na rol mtsho chen po bdun stong yod de/_gnya' shing 'dzin gyi rol mtsho stong dang /_gshol mda' 'dzin gyi stong dang /_seng ldeng can gyi stong dang /_blta na sdug gi stong dang /_rta rna ri'i stong dang /_mu khyud 'dzin gyi stong dang /_rnam par 'dud kyi rol mtsho stong
[\[4a.5\]]rnams so/_/stong spyi phud kyi 'jig rten gyi khams na sems can dmyal ba chen po brgyad stong yod de/_sems can dmyal ba chen po yang sos stong dang /_thig nag stong dang /_bsdus gzhom stong dang /_ngu 'bod stong dang /_ngu 'bod chen po stong dang /_tsha ba stong dang /_rab tu tsha ba stong
[\[4a.6\]]dang /_sems can dmyal ba mnar med pa stong rnams so/_/stong spyi phud kyi 'jig rten gyi khams na sems can gyi gnas dgu stong yod do/_/sems can gzugs yod pa lus tha dad cing 'du shes tha dad pa dag yod de/_'di lta ste/_mi rnams dang /_lha kha cig go/_/'di ni sems
[\[4a.7\]]can gyi gnas dang po'o/_/sems can gzugs yod pa lus tha dad cing 'du shes gcig pa dag yod de/_'di lta ste/_tshangs ris kyi lha dang po byung ba gang yin pa de dag go/_/'di ni sems can gyi gnas gnyis pa'o/_/sems can gzugs yod pa lus gcig la 'du shes tha dad pa
[\[4b\]]
[\[4b.1\]]dag yod de/_'di lta ste/_'od gsal gyi lha rnams so/_/'di ni sems can gyi gnas gsum pa'o/_/sems can gzugs yod pa lus gcig cing 'du shes gcig pa dag yod de/_'di lta ste/_dge rgyas kyi lha rnams so/_/'di ni sems can gyi gnas bzhi pa'o/_/sems
[\[4b.2\]]can gzugs yod pa 'du shes med cing 'du shes dang bral ba dag yod de/_'di lta ste/_'du shes med pa'i lha rnams so/_/'di ni sems can gyi gnas lnga pa'o/_/sems can gzugs med pa rnam pa thams cad du gzugs kyi 'du shes rnams las yang dag par 'das te/_thogs
[\[4b.3\]]pa'i 'du shes rnams nub par gyur cig sna tshogs kyi 'du shes rnams yid la mi byed pas nam mkha' mtha' yas so snyam nas nam mkha' mtha' yas skye mched rdzogs par byas te gnas pa dag yod de/_'di lta ste/_nam mkha' mtha' yas skye mched du skyes pa'i lha rnams so/_/_
[\[4b.4\]]'di ni sems can gyi gnas drug pa'o/_/sems can gzugs med pa rnam pa thams cad du nam mkha' mtha' yas skye mched las yang dag par 'das te/_rnam par shes pa mtha' yas so snyam nas rnam shes mtha' yas skye mched rdzogs par byas te gnas pa dag yod de/_
[\[4b.5\]]'di lta ste/_rnam shes mtha' yas skye mched du skyes pa'i lha rnams so/_/'di ni sems can gyi gnas bdun pa'o/_/sems can gzugs med pa gang dag rnam pa thams cad du rnam shes mtha' yas skye mched las yang dag par 'das te/_ci yang med do snyam nas ci yang med
[\[4b.6\]]pa'i skye mched rdzogs par byas te gnas pa dag yod de/_'di lta ste/_ci yang med pa'i skye mched du skyes pa'i lha rnams so/_/'di ni sems can gyi gnas brgyad pa'o/_/sems can gzugs med pa rnam pa thams cad du ci yang med pa'i skye mched las yang dag par 'das nas
[\[4b.7\]]'du shes med 'du shes med min skye mched rdzogs par byas te gnas pa dag yod de/_'di lta ste/_'du shes med 'du shes med min skye mched du skyes pa'i lha rnams so/_/'di ni sems can gyi gnas dgu pa'o/_/stong spyi phud kyi 'jig rten gyi khams na/_mi dge ba bcu'i las
[\[5a\]]
[\[5a.1\]]kyi lam dag yod de/_srog gcod pa dang /_ma byin par len pa dang /_'dod pa la log par g.yem pa dang /_brdzun du smra ba dang /_phra ma dang /_tshig rtsub po dang /_tshig 'khyal pa dang /_brnab sems dang /_gnod sems dang /_log par lta ba rnams so/_/srog
[\[5a.2\]]gcod pa shas cher kun du bsten cing bsgoms te/_lan mang du byas pas sems can dmyal ba chen po mnar med par skye bar 'gyur ro/_/de bas ches shas chung ba dang /_de bas ches yang bas ni tsha bar ro/_/de bas ches shas chung ba dang /_de bas ches yang bas ni ngu 'bod chen
[\[5a.3\]]por ro/_/de bas ches shas chung ba dang /_de bas ches yang bas ni ngu 'bod du'o/_/de bas ches shas chung ba dang /_de bas ches yang bas ni bsdus gzhom du'o/_/de bas ches shas chung ba dang /_de bas ches yang bas ni thig nag tu'o/_/de bas ches shas chung ba dang /_de bas
[\[5a.4\]]ches yang bas ni sems can dmyal ba chen po yang sos su skye bar 'gyur ro/_/ma byin par len pa shas cher kun tu bsten cing bsgoms te/_lan mang du byas pa dang /_'dod pa la log par g.yem pa dang /_brdzun du smra ba dang /_phra ma dang /_tshig rtsub po dang /_tshig 'khyal pa dang /_
[\[5a.5\]]brnab sems dang /_gnod sems dang /_log par lta ba shas cher kun tu bsten cing bsgoms te/_lan mang du byas pas ni sems can dmyal ba chen po mnar med par skye bar 'gyur ro/_/de bas ches shas chung ba dang /_de bas ches yang bas ni rab tu tsha bar ro/_/de bas shas chung
[\[5a.6\]]ba dang /_de bas ches yang bas ni tsha bar ro/_/de bas ches shas chung ba dang /_de bas ches yang bas ni ngu 'bod chen por ro/_/de bas ches shas chung ba dang /_de bas ches yang bas ni ngu 'bod du'o/_/de bas ches shas chung ba dang /_de bas ches yang bas ni bsdus gzhom du'o/_/de
[\[5a.7\]]bas ches shes chung ba dang /_de bas ches yang bas ni thig nag tu'o/_/de bas ches shas chung ba dang /_de bas ches yang bas ni sems can dmyal ba chen po yang sos su skye bar 'gyur ro/_/'jig rten gzhag pa las tshigs gnyis pa'o/_/mdo la/_mkha' lding las
[\[5b\]]
[\[5b.1\]]lam bcu po dang /_/myong ba dang ni bkres dang zas/_/bdud rtsi phyis char pa dang /_/mu ge bde dang bcu tshan no/_/stong spyi phud kyi 'jig rten gyi khams na klu'i rigs bzhi stong rgya mtsho chen po na gnas so/_/nam mkha' lding gi rigs bzhi stong shing shal ma li mthon po la gnas te/_
[\[5b.2\]]sgo nga las skye ba stong dang /_mngal nas skye ba stong dang /_drod gsher las skye ba stong dang /_rdzus te skye ba stong rnams so/_/nam mkha' lding sgo nga las skye ba ni bza' ba'i phyir klu sgo nga las skye ba 'byin par byed de/_mngal nas skye ba ma yin/_drod gsher las skye ba ma yin/_
[\[5b.3\]]rdzus te skye ba ma yin no/_/de ci'i phyir zhe na/_ci ste de len na/_de nyid thal ba bzhin du byed par 'gyur ba'i phyir ro/_/nam mkha' lding mngal nas skyes pa ni bza' ba'i phyir klu sgo nga las skye ba dang /_mngal nas skye ba 'byin par byed de/_drod gsher las skye ba ma yin/_/rdzus te skye
[\[5b.4\]]ba ma yin no/_/de ci'i phyir zhe na/_ci ste de len na/_de nyid thal ba bzhin du byed par 'gyur ba'i phyir ro/_/nam mkha' lding drod gsher las skye ba ni bza' ba'i phyir klu sgo nga las skye ba dang /_mngal nas skye ba dang /_drod gsher las skye ba 'byin par byed de/_rdzus te skye ba ma yin no/_/_
[\[5b.5\]]de ci'i phyir zhe na/_ci ste de len na de nyid thal ba bzhin du byed par 'gyur ba'i phyir ro/_/nam mkha' lding rdzus te skye ba ni bza' ba'i phyir klu sgo nga las skye ba dang /_mngal nas skye ba dang /_drod gsher las skye ba dang /_rdzus te skye ba 'byin par byed do/_/klu la klu chen po bskal par gnas shing
[\[5b.6\]]sa 'dzin pa dag yod do/_/de dag kyang gang zhe na/_'di lta ste/_klu'i rgyal po dga' bo dang /_nye dga' gnyis dang /_klu'i rgyal po rtas rgyal dang /_klu'i rgyal po btang bzung dang /_klu'i rgyal po gzi can dang /_klu'i rgyal po yul 'khor srung dang /_klu'i rgyal po nag po chen po dang /_
[\[5b.7\]]klu'i rgyal bo e le'i 'dab ma rnams te/_'di dag gzhan yang klu chen po bskal par gnas shing sa 'dzin pa nam mkha' lding dag gis dbyung bar mi nus pa gang yin pa 'di dag ni lha dang lha ma yin gyi g.yul myong bar byed cing so sor myong bar byed de/_shes shing rab tu shes la/_kun
[\[6a\]]
[\[6a.1\]]du rab tu shes so/_/ji skad du/_shin tu mthu che ba yi klu dag yod/_/ma mtha' srung zhing chu na gnas pa ste/_/de dag lha min dag dang g.yul 'gyed pas/_/'di dag brgya byin gyi ni dpung yang yin/_/stobs kyang che zhing dug che klu yin te/_/shin tu drag po
[\[6a.2\]]dgra thabs sna tshogs can/_/lha min rnams dang lhan cig g.yul 'gyed pas/_/de dag brgya byin gyi ni dpung yang yin/_/zhes kyang bya'o/_/bar gyi mdo la/_dga' bo nyer dga' rtas rgyal dang /_/btang bzung dang ni gzi can dang /_/yul 'khor srung dang nag po che/_/e le'i 'dab
[\[6a.3\]]ma phyi ma yin/_/stong spyi phud kyi 'jig rten gyi khams na dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam dag yod de/_srog gcod pa spong ba dang /_ma byin par len pa dang /_'dod pa la log par g.yem pa dang /_brdzun du smra ba dang /_phra ma dang /_tshig rtsub po dang /_tshig 'khyal pa spong ba dang /_brnab
[\[6a.4\]]sems med pa dang /_gnod sems med pa dang /_yang dag par lta ba rnams so/_/srog gcod pa spong ba shas cher kun du bsten cing bsgoms te lan mang du byas pas ni gzhan 'phrul dbang byed kyi lha rnams dang skal ba mnyam par skye bar 'gyur ro/_/de bas ches shas chung ba dang
[\[6a.5\]]de bas ches yang bas ni 'phrul dga' ba rnams so/_/de bas ches shas chung ba dang /_de bas ches yang bas ni dga' ldan pa rnams su'o/_/de bas ches shas chung ba dang /_de bas ches yang bas ni 'thab bral ba rnams su'o/_/de bas ches shas chung ba dang /_de bas ches yang
[\[6a.6\]]bas ni sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams su'o/_/de bas ches shas chung ba dang /_de bas ches yang bas ni rgyal chen bzhi pa rnams su'o/_/de bas ches shas chung ba dang /_de bas ches yang bas ni mi rnams dang skal ba mnyam par skye bar 'gyur ro/_/ma byin par len pa dang /_'dod pa la
[\[6a.7\]]log par g.yem pa dang /_brdzun du smra ba dang /_phra ma dang /_tshig rtsub po dang /_tshig 'khyal pa spong ba dang /_chags sems med pa dang /_gnod sems med pa dang /_yang dag par lta ba shas cher kun tu bsten cing bsgoms te lan mang du byas pas ni gzhan 'phrul dbang byed kyi lha
[\[6b\]]
[\[6b.1\]]rnams dang skal ba mnyam par skye bar 'gyur ro/_/de bas ches shas chung ba dang /_de bas ches yang bas ni 'phrul dga' ba rnams so/_/de bas ches shas chung ba dang /_de bas ches yang bas ni dga' ldan pa rnams su'o/_/de bas ches shas chung ba dang /_de bas ches yang bas ni
[\[6b.2\]]'thab bral ba rnams su'o/_/de bas ches shas chung ba dang /_de bas ches yang bas ni sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams su'o/_/de bas ches shas chung ba dang /_de bas ches yang bas ni rgyal chen bzhi pa rnams su'o/_/de bas ches shas chung ba dang /_de bas ches yang bas ni mi rnams
[\[6b.3\]]dang skal ba mnyam par skye bar 'gyur ro/_/ji ste mi rnams dang skal ba mnyam par skye na yang srog gcod pa spong bas ni tshe ring por 'gyur ro/_/ma byin par len pa spong bas ni longs spyod chen por 'gyur ro/_/'dod pa la log par g.yem pa spong bas ni chung ma 'gran zla med par 'gyur ro/_/_
[\[6b.4\]]brdzun du smra ba spong bas ni skur pa mang bar mi 'gyur ro/_/phra ma spong bas ni mdza' bo dang 'bye bar mi 'gyur ro/_/tshig rtsub po spong bas ni yid du mi 'ong ba'i sgra thos par mi 'gyur ro/_/tshig 'khyal pa spong bas ni tshig mnyan par 'gyur ro/_/chags sems med pas ni 'dod chags
[\[6b.5\]]che bar mi 'gyur ro/_/gnod sems med pas ni zhe sdang che bar mi 'gyur ro/_/yang dag pa'i lta bas ni gti mug che bar mi 'gyur ro/_/sems can dmyal bar myong bar 'gyur ba'i las rnams kyi nang na ni las gang gi rnam par smin pas mnar med pa'i sems can dmyal ba chen po'i che'i
[\[6b.6\]]tshad bskal par len pa 'di mchog yin no/_/dud 'gro myong bar 'gyur ba'i las rnams kyi nang na ni las gang gi rnam par smin pas sa srung gi bus sa srung gi bu nyid dang /_rab tu brtan pas rab tu brtan pa nyid thob pa 'di mchog yin no/_/yi dgas kyi skye gnas su skye bar 'gyur ba'i las
[\[6b.7\]]rnams kyi nang na ni las gang gi rnam par smin pas rgyal po gshin rjes gshin rje'i 'jig rten gyi sems can rnams kyi rgyal srid kyi dbang phyug la dbang byed pa 'di ni mchog yin no/_/mi'i skye gnas myong bar 'gyur ba'i las rnams kyi nang na ni las gang gi rnam par smin pas nga las nus pa
[\[7a\]]
[\[7a.1\]]las nu nyid du thob pa 'di mchog yin no/_/rgyal chen bzhi'i ris myong bar 'gyur ba'i las rnams kyi nang na ni las gang gi rnam par smin pas rgyal po chen po bzhi rnams rgyal srid kyi dbang phyug la dbang byed pa 'di mchog yin no/_/sum cu rtsa gsum myong bar
[\[7a.2\]]'gyur ba'i las rnams kyi nang na ni las gang gi rnam par smin pas brgya byin gyis brgya byin nyid thob pa 'di mchog yin no/_/'thab bral myong bar 'gyur ba'i las rnams kyi nang na ni las gang gi rnam par smin pas rab 'thab bral nyid thob pa 'di mchog yin no/_/dga' ldan myong
[\[7a.3\]]bar 'gyur ba'i las rnams kyi nang na ni las gang gi rnam par smin pas yongs su dga' ldan gyis yongs su dga' ldan nyid thob pa 'di mchog yin no/_/'phrul dga' myong bar 'gyur ba'i las rnams kyi nang na ni las gang gi rnam par smin pas rab sprul nyid thob pa 'di mchog yin no/_/_
[\[7a.4\]]gzhan 'phrul dbang byed myong bar 'gyur ba'i las rnams kyi nang na ni las gang gi rnam par smin pas dbang byed kyi dbang nyid thob pa 'di mchog yin no/_/ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la bkres pa dang /_skom pa yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags po rnams dang /_nub kyi ba
[\[7a.5\]]lang spyod pa rnams dang /_byang gi sgra mi snyan pa rnams dang /_rgyal chen bzhi'i ris kyi lha rnams dang /_sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams dang /_'thab bral ba rnams dang /_dga' ldan pa rnams dang /_'phrul dga' dang /_gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa rnams la yang yod do/_/de phan
[\[7a.6\]]chad la ni bkres pa dang skom pa med do/_/de ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la kha zas 'di lta ste/_'bras chan dang /_zan dang /_phye dang /_sha dang /_khur ba rnams yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags po dang /_nub kyi ba lang spyod la yang yod do/_/byang gi sgra mi snyan gyi mi
[\[7a.7\]]rnams ni ma rmos ma btab pa'i 'bras bu sA lu'i 'bru za'o/_/rgyal chen bzhi'i ris kyi lha rnams ni dri za'i zas dang bdud rtsi'i zas za'o/_/rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams ji lta ba bzhin du sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams dang /_'thab bral ba rnams ba dang /_dga' ldan pa rnams dang /_'phrul
[\[7b\]]
[\[7b.1\]]dga' ba rnams dang /_gzhan 'phrul dbang byed kyi lha rnams kyang de bzhin no/_/de yan chad la ni kham gyi zas med do/_/rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams kyi bdud rtsi ni rnam pa bzhi ste/_sngon po dang /_ser po dang /_dmar po dang /_dkar po rnams so/_/rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams ji
[\[7b.2\]]lta ba bzhin du sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams dang /_'thab bral ba rnams dang /_dga' ldan pa rnams dang /_'phrul dga' ba rnams dang /_gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa rnams kyang de bzhin no/_/tshangs ris pa rnams la ni med do/_/de yan chad la yang med do/_/ji ltar 'dzam bu'i
[\[7b.3\]]gling pa rnams la bshang ba dang gci ba yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags po rnams dang /_nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams dang /_byang gi sgra mi snyan pa rnams la yang yod do/_/rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams la ni med do/_/de yan chad la yang med do/_/ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling
[\[7b.4\]]gi mi rnams la char 'bab mkhas pa dang /_char 'bab mi mkhas pa yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags pa rnams dang /_nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams la yang yod do/_/byang gi sgra mi snyan pa rnams dang /_rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams la ni med do/_/de yan chad la yang med do/_/_
[\[7b.5\]]ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la lo legs pa dang /_mu ge yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags po dang /_nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams la yang yod do/_/byang gi sgra mi snyan pa rnams dang /_rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams la ni med do/_/de yan chad la yang med do/_/ji ltar
[\[7b.6\]]'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la 'jigs pa dang /_bde ba yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags po rnams dang /_nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams la yang yod do/_/byang gi sgra mi snyan gyi mi rnams la ni med do/_/rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams dang /_sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams dang /_'thab
[\[7b.7\]]bral ba rnams dang /_dga' ldan pa rnams dang /_'phrul dga' ba rnams dang /_gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa rnams la yod do/_/tshangs ris pa rnams la ni med do/_/de yan chad la yang med do/_/'jig rten gzhag pa las tshigs gsum pa'o/_/mdo la/_nyo tshong
[\[8a\]]
[\[8a.1\]]mdog dang khang pa dang /_/gding ba dang ni gzhag gos dang /_/yang ba rdul rab bsgre ba dang /_/tha dad bag ma len dang bcu/_/ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la nor ram/_'bru'am/_gser ram dngul nyo tshong bya ba yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags pa rnams dang
[\[8a.2\]]nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams la yang yod do/_/byang gi sgra mi snyan gyi mi rnams dang /_rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams la ni med do/_/de yan chad la yang med do/_/'di snyam du/_'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la nor dang 'bru rnams kyi nyo tshong byed do/_/shar gyi lus 'phags po rnams ni
[\[8a.3\]]ras dang be'u ras rnams kyis so/_/nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams ni ba lang dang nor bu rnams kyis so zhes zer ba yang yod do/_/ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams kyi mdog nag po dang /_dkar po dang /_sngo bsangs dang /_mdog skya snar rnam pa bzhi yod pa bzhin du shar gyi
[\[8a.4\]]lus 'phags pa rnams dang /_nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams kyang de bzhin no/_/byang gi sgra mi snyan gyi mi rnams ni mdog gcig pa ste dkar po'o/_/rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams kyi mdog ni rnam pa bzhi'o/_/sngon po dang /_ser po dang /_dmar po dang /_dkar po rnams so/_/rgyal chen
[\[8a.5\]]bzhi pa rnams kyi ji lta ba bzhin du sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams dang /_'thab bral ba rnams dang /_dga' ldan pa rnams dang /_'phrul dga' ba rnams dang /_gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa rnams kyang de bzhin no/_/tshangs ris kyi lha rnams kyang mdog gcig pa ste dkar po'o/_/tshangs ris
[\[8a.6\]]kyi lha rnams ji lta ba bzhin du tshangs pa'i mdun na 'don pa rnams dang /_tshangs pa chen po pa rnams dang /_'od chung ba rnams dang /_tshad med 'od pa rnams dang /_'od gsal ba rnams dang /_dge chung ba rnams dang /_tshad med dge ba rnams dang /_dge rgyas pa rnams dang /_sprin med pa rnams
[\[8a.7\]]dang /_bsod nams skyes pa rnams dang /_'bras bu che ba rnams dang /_mi che ba rnams dang /_mi gdung ba rnams dang /_gya nom snang ba rnams dang /_shin tu mthong ba rnams dang /_'og min gyi lha rnams kyang de bzhin no/_/nam mkha' mtha' yas skye mched dang /_rnam shes mtha' yas skye

[\[8b.1\]]mched dang /_ci yang med pa'i skye mched dang /_'du shes med 'du shes med min skye mched la ni kha dog med do/_/'di ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams kyi khang pa ched du byas pa dang /_ched du byas pa ma yin pa dang /_khang bzangs dang /_sa khang rnams yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags pa
[\[8b.2\]]rnams dang /_nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams la yang yod do/_/byang gi sgra mi snyan gyi mi rnams kyi khang pa ni ched du byas pa ma yin pa'i sa khang ngo /_/rgyal chen bzhi pa rnams kyi gzhal med khang ni ched du byas pa dang ched du byas pa ma yin pa'o/_/rgyal chen bzhi pa'i lha rnams kyi 'jig rten
[\[8b.3\]]pa bzhin du sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams dang /_'thab bral ba rnams dang /_dga' ldan pa rnams dang /_'phrul dga' ba rnams dang /_gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa rnams kyi yang de bzhin no/_/tshangs ris pa rnams kyi gzhal med khang rnams ni ched du byas pa ma yin pa'o/_/tshangs

[\[8b.6\]]rnams la ni khang pa med pa'o/_/ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la gding ba dang bgo ba 'di lta ste/_bal gos dang /_sha na'i ras dang /_gso ma'i ras dang /_zar ma'i ras dang /_ras gos dang /_zab dar dang /_ko tam pa'i ras dang /_rtswa du ku la'i gos dang /_a pa ra na ti

[\[9a\]]

[\[9b\]]
[\[9b.1\]]par byed do/_/de'i lag tu 'ong bar 'gyur ro/_/rgyal chen bzhi pa rnams kyi ji lta ba bzhin du sum cu rtsa gsum pa dang /_'thab bral ba rnams dang /_dga' ldan ba rnams dang /_'phrul dga' ba rnams dang /_gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa rnams kyi yang de bzhin no/_/tshangs ris kyi lha

[\[10b.5\]]cu rtsa gsum pa rnams dang /_'thab bral ba rnams dang /_dga' ldan pa rnams dang /_'phrul dga' ba rnams dang /_gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa rnams dang /_tshangs ris pa rnams dang /_tshangs pa'i mdun na 'don pa rnams dang /_tshangs pa chen po pa rnams dang /_'od chung ba rnams

[\[14b\]]
[\[14b.1\]]de sum cu la zla ba gcig_/zla ba bcu gnyis la lo gcig ste/_yi dgas rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mtha' ni lo de lta bur brtsis pa'i lo lnga brgya ste/_bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/_/de mi'i ltar brtsis na lo khri lnga stong yod do/_/shar gyi lus 'phags kyi mi rnams kyi che'i tshad kyi

[\[14b.3\]]byang gi sgra mi snyan gyi mi rnams ni bar ma dor 'chi ba med ce na/_/de dag la bdag gi med cing yongs su 'dzin pa med de/_tshe nges shing khyad par du 'gro ba yin pas de'i phyir byang gi sgra mi snyan gyi mi rnams la bar mdor 'chi ba med do/_/'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la ni yar skye ba dang /_mar

[\[14b.5\]]zla ba bcu gnyis la lo gcig ste/_rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mtha' ni lo de lta bur brtsis pa'i lha'i lo lnga brgya ste/_bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/_/de mi'i ltar brtsis na lo sa ya phrag dgu yod do/_/de ni sems can dmyal ba chen po yang sos kyi nyin zhag gcig
[\[14b.6\]]go/_/nyin zhag de sum cu la zla ba gcig_/zla ba bcu gnyis la lo gcig ste/_sems can dmyal ba yang sos kyi sems can rnams kyi che'i tshad kyi mtha' ni de lo lta bur brtsis pa'i sems can dmyal ba pa'i lo lnga brgya ste/_bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/_/de mi'i ltar
[\[14b.7\]]brtsis na lo bye ba phrag 'bum drug khri nyis stong yod do/_/mi rnams kyi lo brgya gang yin pa de ni sum cu rtsa gsum gyi nyin zhag gcig go/_/nyin zhag de sum cu la zla ba gcig_/zla ba bcu gnyis la lo gcig ste/_sum cu rtsa gsum gyi lha rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mtha' ni de lta bur brtsis
[\[15a\]]
[\[15a.1\]]pa'i lha'i lo stong ste/_bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/_/de mi'i ltar brtsis na lo bye ba phrag gsum dang sa ya phrag drug yod do/_/de ni sems can dmyal ba chen po thig nag gi nyin zhag gcig go/_/nyin zhag de sum cu la zla ba gcig go/_/zla ba bcu
[\[15a.2\]]gnyis la lo gcig ste/_sems can dmyal ba chen po thig nag gi che'i tshad kyi mtha' ni lo de lta bur brtsis pa'i sems can dmyal ba'i lo stong ste/_bar mdor 'chi ba ni yod do/_/de mi'i ltar brtsis na lo bye ba phrag 'bum phrag bcu gnyis dang /_bye ba phrag dgu khri drug
[\[15a.3\]]stong yod do/_/mi rnams kyi lo nyis brgya gang yin pa de ni 'thab bral gyi lha rnams kyi nyin zhag gcig go/_/nyin zhag de sum cu la zla ba gcig_/zla ba bcu gnyis la lo gcig ste/_'thab bral ba'i lha rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mtha' ni lo de lta bur brtsis pa'i lha'i lo nyis stong ste/_
[\[15a.4\]]bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/_/de mi'i ltar brtsis na lo bye ba phrag bcu bzhi dang sa ya phrag bzhi yod do/_/de ni sems can dmyal ba chen po bsdus gzhom gyi nyin zhag gcig go/_/nyin zhag de sum cu la zla ba gcig_/zla ba bcu gnyis la lo gcig ste/_sems can dmyal ba
[\[15a.5\]]chen po bsdus gzhom gyi sems can rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mtha' ni lo de lta bur brtsis pa'i sems can dmyal ba'i lo nyis stong ste/_bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/_/de mi'i ltar brtsis na lo bye ba phrag gcig dang /_bye ba phrag gsum 'bum drug khri brgyad stong yod do/_/mi rnams kyi lo bzhi
[\[15a.6\]]brgya gang yin pa de ni dga' ldan gyi lha rnams kyi nyin zhag gcig go/_/nyin zhag sum cu la zla ba gcig_/zla ba bcu gnyis la lo gcig ste/_dga' ldan gyi lha rnams kyi che'i tshad kyi mtha' ni lo de lta bur brtsis pa'i lo bzhi stong yod do/_/bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/_/de mi'i ltar
[\[15a.7\]]brtsis na lo bye ba lnga bcu rtsa bdun dang /_lo sa ya phrag drug yod do/_/de ni sems can dmyal ba chen po ngu 'bod kyi nyin zhag gcig go/_/nyin zhag de sum cu la zla ba gcig_/zla ba bcu gnyis la lo gcig ste/_sems can dmyal ba chen po ngu 'bod kyi sems can rnams kyi tshe'i
[\[15b\]]
[\[15b.1\]]tshad kyi mtha' ni lo de lta bur brtsis pa'i lo bzhi stong ste/_bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/_/de mi'i ltar brtsis na lo bye ba phrag bye ba brgya dang /_bye ba phrag sa ya gnyis dang /_bye ba phrag dgu 'bum bzhi khri bzhi stong yod do/_/mi rnams kyi lo brgyad brgya gang yin pa de ni 'phrul dga' lha
[\[15b.2\]]rnams kyi nyin zhag gcig go/_/nyin zhag de sum cu la zla ba gcig go/_/zla ba bcu gnyis la lo gcig ste/_'phrul dga'i lha rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mtha' ni lo de lta bur brtsis pa'i lha'i lo brgyad stong ste/_bar mdo'i 'chi ba ni yod do/_/de mi'i ltar brtsis na lo bye ba phrag nyis
[\[15b.3\]]brgya sum cu dang /_lo sa ya phrag bzhi yod do/_/de ni sems can dmyal ba chen po ngu 'bod chen po'i nyin zhag gcig go/_/nyin zhag de sum cu la zla ba gcig_/zla ba bcu gnyis la lo gcig ste/_sems can dmyal ba chen po ngu 'bod chen po'i tshe'i tshad kyi mtha' ni lo de lta
[\[15b.4\]]bur brtsis pa'i sems can dmyal ba'i lo brgyad stong yod de/_bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/_/de mi'i ltar brtsis na lo bye ba phrag drug cu rtsa drug dang /_bye ba phrag sa ya gsum dang bye ba phrag lnga 'bum lnga khri nyis stong yod do/_/mi rnams kyi lo stong drug brgya gang yin pa de ni gzhan
[\[15b.5\]]'phrul dbang byed kyi lha rnams kyi nyin zhag gcig go/_/nyin zhag de sum cu la zla ba gcig_/zla ba bcu gnyis la lo gcig ste/_gzhan 'phrul dbang byed kyi lha rnams kyi che'i tshad kyi mtha' ni lo de lta bur brtsis pa'i lha'i lo khri drug stong ste/_bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/_/de mi'i
[\[15b.6\]]ltar brtsis na lo bye ba phrag dgu brgya nyi shu rtsa gcig dang /_lo sa ya drug yod de/_de ni sems can dmyal ba chen po tsha ba'i nyin zhag gcig go/_/nyin zhag de sum cu la zla ba gcig_/zla ba bcu gnyis la lo gcig ste/_sems can dmyal ba chen po tsha ba'i sems can dmyal ba
[\[15b.7\]]pa'i sems can rnams kyi che'i tshad kyi mtha' ni lo de lta bur brtsis pa'i sems can dmyal ba pa'i lo khri drug stong ste/_bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/_/de mi'i ltar brtsis na lo bye ba phrag lnga brgya dang /_lo bye ba phrag bye ba sum cu dang /_lo bye ba phrag sa ya brgyad dang /_bzhi 'bum dang /_lo bye ba
[\[16a\]]
[\[16a.1\]]phrag khri drug stong yod do/_/bar gyi mdo la/_dgu dang gsum dang bcu bzhi dang ni lnga bcu rtsa bdun dang /_/nyis brgya dgu brgya rnams ni mi yi grangs kyi lha tsher bshad/_/de bzhin gcig dang bcu gnyis gcig dang brgyad dang drug cu dang /_/lnga brgya dag ni sems can
[\[16a.2\]]dmyal ba pa yi tsher bshad do/_/tshangs ris kyi lha rnams kyi che'i tshad kyi mtha' ni bskal pa phyed de/_bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/_/sems can dmyal ba chen po rab tu tsha ba'i che'i tshad kyi mtha' ni bskal pa phyed de/_bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/_/tshangs pa'i mdun na 'don pa'i lha
[\[16a.3\]]rnams kyi che'i tshad kyi mtha' ni bskal pa gcig yin te/_bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/_/sems can dmyal ba chen po mnar med pa'i che'i tshad kyi mtha' ni bskal pa gcig ste/_bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/_/tshangs pa chen po pa'i lha rnams kyi che'i tshad kyi mtha' ni bskal pa phyed dang
[\[16a.4\]]gnyis te/_bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/_/'od chung gi lha rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mtha' ni bskal pa gnyis te/_bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/_/tshad med 'od kyi lha rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mtha' ni bskal pa bzhi ste/_bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/_/'od gsal gyi lha rnams kyi che'i tshad kyi
[\[16a.5\]]mtha' ni bskal pa brgyad de/_bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/_/dge chung gi lha rnams kyi che'i tshad kyi mtha' ni bskal pa bcu drug ste/_bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/_/tshad med dge ba'i lha rnams kyi che'i tshad kyi mtha' ni bskal pa sum cu rtsa gnyis te/_bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/_/_
[\[16a.6\]]dge rgyas kyi lha rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mtha' ni bskal pa drug cu rtsa bzhi ste/_bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/_/sprin med kyi lha rnams kyi che'i tshad kyi mtha' ni bskal pa brgya nyi shu rtsa lnga ste/_bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/_/bsod nams skyes kyi lha rnams kyi che'i tshad kyi mtha' ni bskal
[\[16a.7\]]pa nyis brgya lnga bcu ste/_bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/_/'bras bu che ba'i lha rnams kyi che'i tshad kyi mtha' ni bskal pa lnga brgya ste/_bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/_/'du shes med pa'i lha rnams kyang de dang 'dra'o/_/mi che ba'i lha rnams kyi che'i tshad kyi mtha' ni bskal pa stong ste/_
[\[16b\]]
[\[16b.1\]]bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/_/mi gdung ba'i lha rnams kyi che'i tshad kyi mtha' ni bskal pa nyis stong ste/_bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/_/gya nom snang ba'i lha rnams kyi che'i tshad kyi mtha' ni bskal pa bzhi stong ste/_bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/_/shin tu mthong ba'i lha rnams kyi
[\[16b.2\]]tshe'i tshad kyi mtha' ni bskal pa brgyad stong ste/_bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/_/'og min gyi lha rnams kyi che'i tshad kyi mtha' ni bskal pa khri drug stong ste/_bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/_/nam mkha' mtha' yas skye mched pa'i che'i tshad kyi mtha' ni bskal pa nyi khri ste/_bar
[\[16b.3\]]ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/_/rnam shes mtha' yas skye mched pa'i lha rnams kyi che'i tshad kyi mtha' ni bskal pa bzhi khri ste/_bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/_/ci yang med pa'i skye mched kyi lha rnams kyi che'i tshad kyi mtha' ni bskal pa drug khri ste/_bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/_/'du
[\[16b.4\]]shes med 'du shes med min skye mched pa'i lha rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mtha' ni bskal pa brgyad khri ste/_bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/_/'di nas byang phyogs na ri nag po gsum yod do/_/ri nag po gsum po de dag gi byang phyogs na ri nag po gsum yod do/_/ri nag po gzhan gsum po
[\[16b.5\]]de dag gi byang phyogs na yang ri nag po gzhan gsum yod do/_/ri nag po gzhan gsum po de dag gi byang phyogs na ri'i rgyal po gangs zhes bya ba yod do/_/ri'i rgyal po gangs kyi byang phyogs na/_ri'i rgyal po spos kyi ngad ldang zhes bya ba yod do/_/ri'i rgyal po spos kyi ngad ldang nas
[\[16b.6\]]dpag tshad bcu'i tshu rol na mtsho chen po chu zhes bya ba zhig yod de/_ma dros pa zhes kyang bya'o/_/mtsho chen po chu zhes bya ba de la chur dpag tshad lnga bcu zheng du dpag tshad lnga bcu yod do/_/mtha' skor du ni dpag tshad nyis brgya yod do/_/dbyibs legs shing blta na sdug la mdzes
[\[16b.7\]]pa chu bsal zhing chu sbrang rtsi lta bus gang la/_me tog ut+pa la dang /_pad+ma dang /_ku mu ta dang /_pad+ma dkar pos kun du khebs par 'dug go/_/de'i nang nas chu klung chen po bzhi 'di lta ste/_gang+gA dang /_sin+d+hu dang /_si ta dang /_pak+Shu dang /_'di rnams 'bab ste/_gang+gA ni shar
[\[17a\]]
[\[17a.1\]]phyogs nas glang po che'i kha nas 'bab ste/_mtsho chen po chu zhes bya ba'i g.yas phyogs su bskor nas/_klung lnga brgya dang lhan cig tu shar phyogs [(]gyi [,]kyi [)]rgya mtsho chen por 'gro'o/_/sin+d+hu ni lho phyogs nas khyu mchog gi kha nas 'bab ste/_de ni mtsho chen po chu zhes bya ba'i g.yas
[\[17a.2\]]phyogs su bskor nas klung lnga brgya dang lhan cig tu lho phyogs kyi rgya mtsho chen por 'gro'o/_/pak+Shu ni nub phyogs nas rta'i kha nas 'bab ste/_de ni mtsho chen po chu zhes bya ba'i g.yas phyogs su bskor nas/_klung lnga brgya dang lhan cig tu nub phyogs kyi rgya mtsho chen por 'gro'o/_/si ta ni byang
[\[17a.3\]]phyogs nas seng ge'i kha nas 'bab ste/_de ni mtsho chen po chu zhes bya ba'i g.yas phyogs su bskor nas/_klung lnga brgya dang lhan cig tu byang phyogs kyi rgya mtsho chen por 'gro'o/_/'di skad du/_byang phyogs kha dgur 'gyur ba yi/_/chu mtsho yod de gzhan dag kyang /_/de ni mtsho chen chu
[\[17a.4\]]zhes bya/_/tha dad rgyu rnams 'byung gnas yod/_/chu klung gang+gA sin+d+hu pak+Shu dang /_/si ta dba' rlabs lbu ba'i phreng ba can/_/'bab cing thams cad gsal ba'i chu yin te/_/phyogs bzhi kho ra khor yug dag nas 'byung /_/gang+gA shar phyogs rgya mtshor 'gro ba ste/_/sin+d+hu lho phyogs rgya
[\[17a.5\]]mtshor 'gro ba yin/_/pak+Shu yang ni nub phyogs rgya mtshor 'gro/_/de yi byang phyogs rgya mtshor si ta 'gro/_/chu klung rab mchog bzhi po 'di dag ni/_/mchog tu bzang zhing so sor 'bab pa ste/_/re re zhing yang lnga brgya khyer nas ni/_/chu yi rgyun rnams rgya mtsho chen por 'gro/_/zhes kyang bya'o/_/_
[\[17a.6\]]ri spos kyi ngad ldang de'i byang phyogs dpag tshad nyi shu na gser gyi brag bya skyibs lha ma yin gyi ngos zhes bya ba yod de/_chur dpag tshad lnga bcu zhing du yang dpag tshad lnga bcu/_mtha' skor du dpag tshad nyis brgya 'phang du dpag tshad phyed dang bzhi yod pa/_dbyibs legs shing blta na
[\[17a.7\]]sdug la mdzes pa zhig yod do/_/de'i nang gis gzhi yang dbyibs legs shing blta na sdug la/_mdzes pa gser gyi bye ma bdal zhing tsan+dan gyi chus chag chag btab pa ste/_der yid du mi 'ong ba shing ngam/_/gseg ma 'am/_gang ci yang rung ba dag lhung na de mi ma yin pa
[\[17b\]]
[\[17b.1\]]rnams kyi rlung gi mthus phyi rol du gtor ro/_/de'i kho ra khor yug na gser gyi brag bya skyibs can brgya stong yod do/_/de dag thams cad kyang dbyibs legs shing blta na sdug la mdzes pa ste/_de dag gi nang nas gzhi rnams kyang dbyibs legs shing blta na sdug la/_mdzes
[\[17b.2\]]pa gser gyi phye ma bdal zhing tsan+dan gyi chus chag chag btab pa/_de dag tu yang yid du mi 'ong ba shing ngam/_gseg ma 'am/_gang ci yang rung ba dag lhung na/_de mi ma yin pa rnams kyi rlung gi mthus phyi rol du 'dor ro/_/de'i lam srid du dpag tshad nyi shu/_zheng du dpag
[\[17b.3\]]tshad phyed dang gnyis yod pa dbyibs legs shing blta na sdug la mdzes pa gser gyi phye ma bdal zhing tsan+dan gyi chus chag chag btab pa zhig yod de/_de yang yid du mi 'ong ba shing ngam gseg ma'am/_gang ci yang rung ba dag lhung na de mi ma yin pa rnams kyi rlung gi mthus phyi rol
[\[17b.4\]]du 'dor ro/_/brag bya skyibs lha ma yin gyi ngos de'i byang phyogs dpag tshad nyi shu na shing sA la'i rgyal po chen po rab tu brtan pa zhes bya ba sA la'i phreng ba rim pa bdun gyis bskor ba zhig yod do/_/sA la'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pa de'i rtsa ba ni 'dom bcu bzhi thur du zug go/_/sA la'i
[\[17b.5\]]phreng ba dang po'i rtsa ba ni 'dom bcu gsum thur du zug go/_/gnyis pa'i ni bcu gnyis so/_/gsum pa'i ni bcu gcig go/_/bzhi pa'i ni bcu'o/_/lnga pa'i ni dgu'o/_/drug pa'i ni brgyad do/_/sA la'i phreng ba bdun pa'i rtsa ba ni 'dom bdun thur du zug go/_/sA la'i rgyal po rab
[\[17b.6\]]tu brtan pa de'i yal ga dang /_lo ma dang yal ga rnams gang yin pa de ni sA la'i phreng ba dang po la thug go/_/sA la'i phreng ba dang po ni yal ga dang lo ma dang yal ga gang yin pa de ni gnyis pa la'o/_/gnyis pa'i gang yin pa de ni gsum pa la'o/_/gsum pa'i gang yin pa de ni bzhi
[\[17b.7\]]pa la'o/_/bzhi pa'i gang yin pa de ni lnga pa la'o/_/lnga pa'i gang yin pa de ni drug pa la'o/_/drug pa'i gang yin pa de ni bdun pa la'o/_/sA la'i phreng ba bdun pa'i yal ga dang /_lo ma dang yal ga gang yin pa de ni nam mkha' khyab par 'dug go/_/de'i nang gi sa gzhi yang
[\[18a\]]
[\[18a.1\]]dbyibs legs shing blta na sdug la/_mdzes pa gser gyi phye ma bdal zhing tsan+dan gyi chus chag chag btab pa ste/_de yang yid du mi 'ong ba shing ngam gseg ma'am/_gang ci yang rung ba dag lhung na ni de mi ma yin pa rnams kyi rlung gi mthus phyi rol tu 'dor
[\[18a.2\]]ro/_/de'i lam srid du dpag tshad nyi shu/_zheng du dpag tshad phyed dang gnyis yod pa/_dbyibs legs shing blta na sdug la mdzes pa zhig yod do/_/der yang yid du mi 'ong ba shing ngam gseg ma'am gang ci yang rung ba dag lhung na de mi ma yin pa rnams kyi rlung gi mthus phyi rol
[\[18a.3\]]du 'dor ro/_/sA la'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pa'i shar phyogs dpag tshad nyi shu na/_rdzing bu dal gyis 'bab ces bya ba chur dpag tshad lnga bcu/_zheng du yang dpag tshad lnga bcu ste/_mtha' skor du dpag tshad nyis brgya yod pa/_dbyibs legs shing blta na sdug la mdzes pa chu
[\[18a.4\]]bsil zhing chu sbrang rtsi lta bus gang ba/_me tog ut+pa la dang /_pad+ma dang /_ku mu ta dang /_pad+ma dkar pos khebs pa zhig yod do/_/rdzing bu dal gyis 'bab pa de'i nang gi pad+ma'i lo ma rnams che zhing mchog tu che ste/_'di lta ste/_ba lang gi ko ba tsam mo/_/pad+ma'i sdong bu rnams che zhing mchog
[\[18a.5\]]tu che ste/_'di lta ste/_gshol mda' tsam mo/_/pad+ma'i me tog rnams che zhing mchog tu che ste/_'di lta ste/_shing rta'i 'phang lo tsam mo/_/pad+ma'i rtsa ba rnams che zhing mchog tu che ste/_'di lta ste/_skyes bu chen po'i brla tsam mo/_/ro mngar zhing mchog tu mngar ste/_'di lta ste/_sbrang
[\[18a.6\]]bu'i sbrang rtsi ma bskol ba bzhin no/_/bcad na yang 'o ma 'dzag go/_/rdzing bu dal gyis 'bab kyi kho ra khor yug na rdzing bu brgyad stong yod de/_de dag thams cad kyang dbyibs legs shing blta na sdug la mdzes pa chu bsil zhing sbrang rtsi lta bus gang ngo /_/de dag gi nang gi pad+ma'i lo ma
[\[18a.7\]]rnams kyang che zhing mchog tu che ste/_'di lta ste/_ba lang gi ko ba tsam mo/_/pad+ma'i sdong bu rnams che zhing mchog tu che ste/_'di lta ste/_gshol mda' tsam mo/_/pad+ma'i me tog rnams che zhing mchog tu che ste/_'di lta ste/_shing rta'i 'phang lo tsam mo/_/pad+ma'i rtsa ba rnams che zhing
[\[18b\]]
[\[18b.1\]]mchog tu che ste/_'di lta ste/_skyes bu chen po'i brla tsam mo/_/ro mngar zhing mchog tu mngar te/_'di lta ste/_sbrang bu'i sbrang rtsi ma bskol ba bzhin no/_/bcad na yang 'o ma 'dzag go/_/de'i lam srid du dpag tshad nyi shu/_zhing du dpag tshad phyed dang gnyis yod pa/_
[\[18b.2\]]dbyibs legs shing blta na sdug la mdzes pa gser gyi phye ma bdal zhing tsan+dan gyi chus chag chag btab pa zhig yod de/_der yang yid du mi 'ong ba shing ngam/_gseg ma'am/_gang ci yang rung bdag lhung na de mi ma yin pa rnams kyi rlung gi mthus phyi rol du 'dor ro/_/_
[\[18b.3\]]sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kyi glang po che'i rgyal po g.yul dor chas pa rab tu brtan pa zhes bya ba gzugs bzang zhing blta na sdug la mdzes pa zhig yod de/_me tog ku mu ta'i mdog ltar thal kar du 'dug la/_yan lag bdun shin tu legs par gnas pa ste/_
[\[18b.4\]]de mgo bo yang dbyibs legs shing blta na sdug la mdzes pa ste/_sngo zhing srog chags lham bu chug sher gyi mdog ltar dbus dmar la mche ba drug yod de/_glang po che rab tu brtan pa srid du dpag tshad phyed dang gsum/_zheng du dpag tshad gcig 'phang du dpag tshad phyed
[\[18b.5\]]dang gnyis/_mtha' skor du dpag tshad bdun yod do/_/de'i 'khor glang po che brgyad stong yod do/_/de thams cad kyang gzugs bzang zhing blta na sdug pa mdzes pa/_me tog ku mu ta'i mdog ltar thal kar du 'dug cing yan lag bdun shin tu legs par gnas pa ste/_de
[\[18b.6\]]dag gi mgo bo yang dbyibs legs shing blta na sdug la mdzes pa ste/_sngo zhing srog chags lham bu chu gsher gyi mdog ltar dbus dmar la mche ba drug yod pa sha stag ste/_glang po che'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pa de 'khor dang bcas pa dgun zla ba bzhi ni brag bya
[\[18b.7\]]skyibs lha ma yin gyi ngos kyi nang na gnas shing 'khod do/_/dpyid zla ba bzhi ni shing sA la'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pa'i nang na gnas shing 'khod do/_/dbyar zla ba bzhi ni rdzing bu dal gyis 'bab kyi nang na gnas shing 'khod do/_/gang gi tshe glang po che'i rgyal po rab tu brtan
[\[19a\]]
[\[19a.1\]]pa brag bya skyibs lha ma yin gyi ngos kyi nang na gnas shing 'dug pa de'i tshe ni glang po che brgyad stong po rnams 'di lta ste/_glang po che'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pa srung ba dang sba ba dang mdzes par bya ba'i phyir brag bya skyibs brgyad stong gi nang na nye bar gnas shing 'khod
[\[19a.2\]]do/_/gang gi tshe glang po che'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pa brag bya skyibs lha ma yin gyi ngos kyi nang na gnas shing sA la'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pa'i nang du 'gro ba na/_res 'ga' ni tha mal pa'i tshul gyis 'gro'o/_/res 'ga' ni 'di lta ste/_lha dang lha'i bu rdzu 'phrul che zhing gang yang rung ba
[\[19a.3\]]dang 'dra bar bdag nyid mngon par sprul nas glang po che thams cad kyi nang na dbang che bar grags pa gang yin pa de nyid kyi mgo bo'am/_rgyab tu zhon te sil snyan dang pheg rdob pa dag cher byed cing 'gro'o/_/gang gi tshe glang po che'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pa'i nang na gnas shing 'dug pa de'i tshe ni
[\[19a.4\]]glang po che brgyad stong po 'di dag kyang 'di lta ste/_glang po che'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pa srung ba dang /_spa ba dang /_mdzes par bya ba'i phyir shing sA la'i phreng ba rim pa bdun po dag gi nang na kha nang du bltas shing 'khod do/_/shing sA la'i phreng ba dang po'i nang na 'dug pa gang yin pa de dag
[\[19a.5\]]kyang kha nang du bltas te 'khod do/_/gnyis pa'i nang na 'dug pa gang yin pa de dag kyang kha nang du lta'o/_/gsum pa'i nang du 'dug pa gang yin pa de dag kyang kha nang du lta'o/_/bzhi pa'i nang du 'dug pa de dag kyang kha nang du lta'o/_/lnga pa'i nang na 'dug pa gang yin pa de dag kyang
[\[19a.6\]]kha nang du lta'o/_/drug pa'i nang na 'dug pa gang yin pa de dag kyang kha nang du lta'o/_/bdun pa'i nang na 'dug pa gang yin pa de dag kyang kha nang du bltas te 'khod do/_/gang gi tshe glang po che'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pa shing sA la'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pa nas rdzing bu dal gyis 'bab par
[\[19a.7\]]'gro ba na/_res 'ga' ni tha mal pa'i tshul gyis 'gro'o/_/res 'ga' ni 'di lta ste/_lha'am lha'i bu rdzu 'phrul che zhing mthu che ba gang yang rung ba dang 'dra bar bdag nyid mngon par sprul nas glang po che de dag thams cad kyi nang na dbang che bar grags pa gang yin pa de nyid kyi mgo
[\[19b\]]
[\[19b.1\]]'am/_rgyab tu zhon te sil snyan dang pheg rdob pa dag rgya cher byed cing 'gro'o/_/gang gi tshe glang po che'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pa rdzing bu dal gyis 'bab kyi nang du zhugs nas rtse zhing dga' la dga' dgur spyod pa de'i tshe glang po che brgyad stong po de dag 'di lta ste/_glang po che'i rgyal po rab tu brtan
[\[19b.2\]]pa de srung ba dang /_sba ba dang /_mdzes par bya ba'i phyir rdzing bu dal gyis 'bab kyi mtha' kho ra khor yug nas bskor te kha nang du bltas shing 'khod do/_/gang gi tshe glang po che'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pa rdzing bu dal gyis 'bab kyi nang nas rtse zhing dga' la dga' mgur spyad nas phyir byung ba de'i tshe nang
[\[19b.3\]]na glang po che dbang che bar grags pa gang yin pa de rdzing bu dal gyis 'bab kyi nang du zhugs nas pad+ma'i rtsa ba rnams blangs te/_shin tu bkrus shing rab tu bshal nas glang po che'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pa la 'bul lo/_/gang gi tshe glang po che'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pas zos shing 'thungs te
[\[19b.4\]]'grangs par gyur pa de'i tshe glang po che gzhan brgyad stong po de dag kyang rdzing bu brgyad stong gi nang na rdzing bu re re zhugs na rtse zhing dga' la dga' dgur spyod do/_/pad+ma'i rtsa ba dag blangs nas shin tu bkrus shing rab tu bshal te za'o/_/sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kyi glang po che rgyal po
[\[19b.5\]]g.yul ngor spyad pa rab tu bstan pa'i mthu ni de tsam mo/_/sems can thams cad ni srung ma dang bcas shing srung ba dang /_skyob pa dang sbed pa dang /_mi 'bral ste/_sems can gang dbang chung bar grags shing bsod nams chung la/_gzi brjid chung ba de dag ni brgya phrag mang po dang /_stong phrag
[\[19b.6\]]mang po la gcig srung ste/_dper na ba lang ngam lug brgya phrag mang po dang stong phrag mang po la gcig srung ba de bzhin du/_sems can gang dbang chung bar grags shing bsod nams chung la/_gzi brjid chung ba de dag ni brgya phrag mang po dang /_stong phrag mang po la gcig bsrung ngo /_/_
[\[19b.7\]]sems can gang dbang che bar grags shing bsod nams che la gzi brjid che ba de dag ni brgya phrag mang po dang /_stong phrag mang po dag gis gcig tu bsrung ste/_dper na 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po'am/_de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas
[\[20a\]]
[\[20a.1\]]la brgya phrag mang po dang /_stong phrag mang po dag gis gcig tu srung ba de bzhin du sems can gang dbang che bar grags shing bsod nams che la gzi brjid che ba de dag la brgya phrag mang po dang /_stong phrag mang po dag gis gcig tu srung ngo /_/'dir smras pa/_
[\[20a.2\]]ji ste sems can thams cad srung ma dang bcas shing srung ba dang /_skyob pa dang /_sbed pa dang mi 'bral na ci'i phyir 'tshe ba yod par 'gyur/_smras pa/_srung ma mthu chung ba zhig yin na de la zil gyis gnon pa la 'tshe ba yod do/_/srung ma bag med cing bag med par gnas pa
[\[20a.3\]]zhig yin na ni bag med pa'i rgyu las kyang 'tshe ba rnams yod do/_/srung ma gnyis lhan cig mthun par gyur pas kyang zil gyis mnan nas 'tshe bar byed do/_/mi rnams chos ma yin pa spyod cing mi rigs pa spyod pa zhig yin na de dag gis chos ma yin pa spyod pa dang /_mi rigs pa
[\[20a.4\]]spyod pa las kyang 'tshe ba yod do//_//'jig rten gzhag pa/_bam po gsum pa/_sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kyi mi rnams kyi srung ma 'di lta ste/_lam po che dang /_srang dang /_bzhi mdo dang /_sum mdo dang /_dri 'tshong ba'i gnas rnams dang /_me tog
[\[20a.5\]]phreng ba 'tshong ba'i gnas rnams dang /_zong dgram pa'i gnas rnams dang /_btung ba 'tshong ba'i gnas rnams dang /_rtag tu myos pa'i gnas rnams dang /_gsod byed kyi gnas su bkod pa dag yod de/_zla ba phyed kyi tshes brgyad la rgyal po chen po bzhi po dag gi g.yog zho shas
[\[20a.6\]]'tsho ba rnams kyis lam po che dang /_srang dang /_bzhi mdo dang /_sum mdo dang /_dri 'tshong ba'i gnas rnams dang /_me tog gi phreng ba 'tshong ba'i gnas rnams dang /_zong dgram pa'i gnas rnams dang /_btung ba 'tshong ba'i gnas rnams dang /_rtag tu myos pa'i gnas rnams dang /_
[\[20a.7\]]gsod byed kyi gnas rnams na su zhig 'dug ces 'jig rten 'di thams cad byul te/_ci ste de dag gis skyen par tshor na ni de dag gnas mthon po la 'god do/_/ji ste de dag gis skyen par ma tshor ba na ni de dag gnas dma' ba la 'god do/_/zla ba phyed kyi tshes bcu bzhi la ni rgyal po chen
[\[20b\]]
[\[20b.1\]]po bzhi po de dag gi bu rnams kyi lam po che dang /_srang dang /_bzhi mdo dang /_sum mdo dang /_dri 'tshong ba'i gnas rnams dang /_me tog gi phreng ba 'tshong ba'i gnas rnams dang /_zong dgram pa'i gnas rnams dang /_btung ba 'tshong ba'i gnas rnams dang /_rtag tu myos pa'i gnas
[\[20b.2\]]rnams dang /_gsod byed kyi gnas rnams na su zhig 'dug ces 'jig rten 'di thams cad byul te/_ci ste de dag gis skyen par tshor na ni/_de dag gnas mthon po la 'god do/_/ci ste de dag gis skyen par ma tshor na ni de dag gnas dma' ba la 'god do/_/zla ba phyed kyi tshe bcu lnga la
[\[20b.3\]]ni rgyal po chen po bzhi po de dag nyid kyi lam po che dang /_srang dang /_bzhi mdo dang /_sum mdo dang /_dri 'tshong ba'i gnas rnams dang /_me tog gi phreng ba 'tshong ba'i gnas rnams dang /_zong dgram pa'i gnas rnams dang /_btung ba 'tshong ba'i gnas rnams dang /_rtag tu myos pa'i gnas
[\[20b.4\]]rnams dang /_gsod byed kyi gnas rnams na su zhig 'dug ces 'jig rten 'di thams cad byul te/_ci ste de dag gis skyen par tshor na ni/_de dag gnas mthon po la 'god do/_/ci ste de dag gis skyen par ma tshor na ni de dag gnas dma' ba la 'god do/_/bcom ldan 'das kyis kyang
[\[20b.5\]]'di skad du dge slong dag zla ba phyed kyi tshes brgyad la ni rgyal po chen po bzhi po dag gi zho shas 'tsho ba rnams ni ci mi dang mi ma yin pa'i 'jig rten na mar 'dzin pa dang /_phar 'dzin pa dang /_dge sbyong du 'dzin pa dang /_bram zer 'dzin pa dang /_rigs kyi nang na rgan rabs la rim gro byed pa dang /_
[\[20b.6\]]don byed pa dang /_bya ba'i rigs pa byed pa dang /_bsod nams byed pa dang /_tshe 'di dang tshe phyi ma la kha na ma tho ba rnams kyis 'jigs par lta ba dang /_sbyin pa dag sbyin zhing bsod nams dag byed pa dang /_gso sbyong la nye bar gnas pa dang /_tshul khrims yang dag par blangs
[\[20b.7\]]nas 'dug pa dag mang ngam zhes 'jig rten 'di thams cad du nyul lo/_/zla ba phyed kyi tshes bcu bzhi la ni rgyal po chen po bzhi po dag gi bu rnams ci mi dang mi ma yin pa'i 'jig rten na mar 'dzin pa dang /_phar 'dzin pa dang /_dge sbyong du 'dzin pa dang /_bram zer 'dzin pa dang /_rigs kyi
[\[21a\]]
[\[21a.1\]]nang na rgan rabs la rim gro byed pa dang /_don byed pa dang /_bya ba'i rigs pa byed pa dang /_bsod nams byed pa dang /_tshe 'di dang tshe phyi ma la kha na ma tho ba rnams kyis 'jigs par lta ba dang /_sbyin pa dag sbyin zhing /_bsod nams dag byed pa dang /_gso
[\[21a.2\]]sbyong la nye bar gnas pa dang /_tshul khrims yang dag par blangs nas 'dug pa dag mang ngam zhes 'jig rten 'di dag thams cad nyul lo/_/zla ba phyed kyi tshes bcwa lnga la ni rgyal bo chen po bzhi po de dag nyid ci mi dang mi ma yin pa'i 'jig rten na mar 'dzin pa dang /_phar 'dzin pa dang /_
[\[21a.3\]]dge sbyong du 'dzin pa dang /_bram zer 'dzin pa dang /_rigs kyi nang na rgan rabs la rim gro byed pa dang /_don byed pa dang /_bya ba'i rigs pa byed pa dang /_bsod nams byed pa dang /_tshe 'di dang tshe phyi ma la kha na ma tho ba rnams kyis 'jigs par lta ba dang /_sbyin pa dag sbyin zhing bsod
[\[21a.4\]]nams dag byed pa dang /_gso sbyong la nye bar gnas pa dang /_tshul khrims yang dag par blangs nas 'dug pa dag mang ngam zhes 'jig rten 'di thams cad nyul lo/_/ci ste mi dang mi ma yin pa'i 'jig rten na mar mi 'dzin pa dang /_phar mi 'dzin pa dang /_dge sbyong du mi 'dzin pa dang /_
[\[21a.5\]]bram zer mi 'dzin pa dang /_rigs kyi nang na rgan rabs la rim gro mi byed pa dang /_don mi byed pa dang /_bya ba'i rigs pa dag mi byed pa dang /_bsod nams mi byed pa dang /_tshe 'di dang tshe phyi ma la kha na ma tho ba rnams kyis 'jigs par mi lta ba dang /_sbyin pa dag mi sbyin zhing bsod
[\[21a.6\]]nams dag mi byed pa dang /_gso sbyong la nye bar mi gnas pa dang /_tshul khrims yang dag par blangs te/_mi 'dug pa dag mang na ni rgyal po chen po bzhi po rnams sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams lha'i 'dun sa chos bzangs su 'dus shing 'khod pa'i nang du song nas 'di skad du
[\[21a.7\]]grogs po dag 'di shes par gyis shig_/mi dang mi ma yin pa'i 'jig rten na mar mi 'dzin pa dang /_phar mi 'dzin pa dang /_dge sbyong du mi 'dzin pa dang /_bram zer mi 'dzin pa dang /_rigs kyi nang na rgan rabs la rim gro mi byed pa dang /_don mi byed pa dang /_bya ba'i rigs
[\[21b\]]
[\[21b.1\]]pa dag mi byed pa dang /_bsod nams mi byed pa dang /_tshe 'di dang tshe phyi ma la kha na ma tho ba rnams kyis 'jigs par mi lta ba dang /_sbyin pa dag mi sbyin zhing bsod nams dag mi byed pa dang /_gso sbyong la nye bar mi gnas pa dang /_tshul khrims yang dag par blangs te mi 'dug pa dag
[\[21b.2\]]mang ngo zhes bsnyad do/_/de dag las thos nas sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams yi ma rangs shing mi mgu bar gyur nas yi ma rangs pa nyid kyang phyir zlog par byed de/_/kye ma grogs po dag 'di ltar mi dang mi ma yin pa'i 'jig rten na mar mi 'dzin pa dang /_phar mi 'dzin ba dang /_
[\[21b.3\]]dge sbyong du mi 'dzin pa dang /_bram zer mi 'dzin pa dang /_rigs kyi nang na rgan rabs la rim gror mi byed pa dang /_don mi byed pa dang /_bya ba'i rigs pa mi byed pa dang /_bsod nams mi byed pa dang /_tshe 'di dang tshe phyi ma la kha na ma tho ba rnams kyis 'jigs par mi lta ba dang /_
[\[21b.4\]]sbyin pa dag mi sbyin zhing bsod nams dag mi byed pa dang /_gso sbyong la nye bar mi gnas pa dang /_tshul khrims yang dag par blangs te/_mi 'dug pa mang ba ni mi rnams kyi chos mdzes pa ma yin no/_/rkyen du bab pa ma yin no/_/legs pa ma yin no/_/dge ba ma yin no/_/de
[\[21b.5\]]ltar na lha rnams kyi tshogs ni yongs su 'grib par 'gyur la/_lha ma yin rnams kyi tshogs ni mngon par 'phel bar 'gyur ro zhes zlos so/_/ji ste mi dang mi ma yin pa'i 'jig rten na mar 'dzin pa dang /_phar 'dzin pa dang /_dge sbyong du 'dzin pa dang /_bram zer 'dzin pa dang /_rigs kyi
[\[21b.6\]]nang na rgan rabs la rim gro byed pa dang /_don byed pa dang /_bya ba'i rigs pa byed pa dang /_bsod nams byed pa dang /_tshe 'di dang tshe phyi ma dang kha na ma tho ba rnams kyis 'jigs par lta ba dang /_sbyin pa dag sbyin zhing bsod nams dag byed pa dang /_gso sbyong la nye bar gnas pa dang /_tshul
[\[21b.7\]]khrims yang dag par blangs nas 'dug pa dag mang na ni rgyal po chen po bzhi po rnams sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams lha'i mdun sa chos bzangs du 'dus shing 'khod pa'i nang du song nas 'di skad du grogs po dag 'di shes par gyis shig_/mi dang mi ma yin pa'i 'jig rten na mar 'dzin pa dang /_
[\[22a\]]
[\[22a.1\]]phar 'dzin pa dang /_dge sbyong du 'dzin pa dang /_bram zer 'dzin pa dang /_rigs kyi nang na rgan rabs la rim gro byed pa dang /_don byed pa dang /_bya ba'i rigs pa byed pa dang /_bsod nams byed pa dang /_tshe 'di dang tshe phyi ma la kha na ma tho ba rnams kyis 'jigs par
[\[22a.2\]]lta ba dang /_sbyin pa dag sbyin zhing bsod nams dag byed pa dang /_gso sbyong la nye bar gnas pa dang /_tshul khrims yang dag par blangs nas 'dug pa dag mang ngo zhes bsnyad na ni de dag las thos nas sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams yi rangs shing mgu bar gyur nas yi rangs ba nyid
[\[22a.3\]]kyang zlos par byed de/_kye ma'o grogs po dag 'di ltar mi dang mi ma yin pa'i 'jig rten na mar 'dzin pa dang /_phar 'dzin pa dang /_dge sbyong du 'dzin pa dang /_bram zer 'dzin pa dang /_rigs kyi nang na rgan rabs la rim gro byed pa dang /_don byed pa dang /_bya ba'i rigs pa byed
[\[22a.4\]]pa dang /_bsod nams byed pa dang /_tshe 'di dang tshe phyi ma la kha na ma tho ba rnams kyis 'jigs par lta ba dang /_sbyin pa dag sbyin zhing bsod nams dag byed pa dang /_gso sbyong la nye bar gnas pa dang /_tshul khrims yang dag par blangs nas 'dug pa dag mang ba ni mi rnams kyi chos
[\[22a.5\]]mdzes so/_/rkyen du bab bo/_/legs so/_/dge'o/_/de ltar na lha rnams kyi tshogs ni mngon par 'phel bar 'gyur la/_lha ma yin gyi tshogs ni yongs su 'grib par 'gyur ro zhes zlos so/_/de nas lha rnams kyi dbang po brgya byin gyis lha'i 'khor rab tu dga' la bde zhing
[\[22a.6\]]yid bde ba skyes par rig nas/_de'i tshe tshigs su bcad de smras pa/_'di ni zla phyed tshes brgyad dang /_/de bzhin bcu bzhi bco lnga dang /_/cho 'phrul gyi ni zla phyed la 'ang /_/gso sbyong yan lag brgyad pa la/_/shin tu mnyam gzhag gnas byed 'dir/_/nga ci 'dra bar de bzhin 'gyur/_/_
[\[22a.7\]]dge slong dag lha rnams kyi dbang po brgya byin gyis gang 'di skad du/_'dir ni zla phyed tshes brgyad dang /_/de bzhin bcu bzhi bco lnga dang /_/cho 'phrul gyi ni zla phyed la'ang /_/gso sbyong yan lag brgyad pa la/_/shin tu mnyam gzhag gnas byed 'dir/_/nga ci 'dra bar de bzhin 'gyur/_/zhes
[\[22b\]]
[\[22b.1\]]tshigs su bcad pa smras pa de ni nyes par smras pa yin gyi legs par smras pa ma yin no/_/nyes par bstod pa yin gyi/_legs par bstod pa ma yin no/_/nyes par brjod pa yin gyi legs par brjod pa ma yin no/_/dge slong dag de ci'i phyir zhe na/_lha'i dbang po brgya byin
[\[22b.2\]]de ni 'dod chags dang bcas pa/_zhe sdang dang bcas pa/_gti mug dang bcas pa ste/_skye ba dang /_rga ba dang /_na ba dang /_'chi ba dang /_mya ngan dang /_smre sngags 'don pa dang /_sdug bsngal ba dang /_yid mi bde ba dang /_'khrugs pa rnams las yongs su ma grol zhing
[\[22b.3\]]sdug bsngal las yongs su ma grol lo zhes nga smra'o/_/de bas na des gang 'di skad du/_'dir ni zla phyed tshes brgyad dang /_/de bzhin bcu bzhi bco lnga dang /_/cho 'phrul gyi ni zla phyed la'ang /_/gso sbyong yan lag brgyad pa dang /_/shin tu mnyam gzhag gnas byed 'dir/_/_
[\[22b.4\]]nga ci 'dra ba de bzhin 'gyur/_/zhes tshigs su bcad pas smras pa 'di nyes par smras pa yin gyi legs par smras pa ma yin no/_/nyes par bstod pa yin gyi legs par bstod pa ma yin no/_/nyes par brjod pa yin gyi legs par brjod pa ma yin no/_/dge slong dag dge slong gang dgra
[\[22b.5\]]bcom pa yin zhing zag pa zad pa/_bya ba byas pa/_byed pa byas pa/_khur bor ba/_bdag gi don rjes su thob pa/_srid pa kun tu sbyor ba/_yongs su zad pa/_yang dag pa'i shes pas sems shin tu rnam par grol ba des ni gang 'di skad du/_'dir ni zla phyed tshes brgyad dang /_/de bzhin
[\[22b.6\]]bcu bzhi bco lnga dang /_/cho 'phrul gyi ni zla phyed la'ang /_/gso sbyong yan lag brgyad pa la/_/shin tu mnyam gzhag gnas byed 'dir/_/nga ci 'dra bar de bzhin 'gyur/_/zhes tshigs su bcad pa 'di smras na legs par smras pa yin te nyes par smras pa ma yin no/_/legs par bstod pa
[\[22b.7\]]yin te/_/nyes par bstod pa ma yin no/_/legs par brjod pa yin te nyes par brjod pa ma yin no/_/dge slong dag de ci'i phyir zhe na/_dge slong de ni 'dod chags dang bral ba/_zhe sdang dang bral ba/_gti mug dang bral ba ste/_skye ba dang /_rga ba dang /_na ba dang /_'chi ba dang /_mya
[\[23a\]]
[\[23a.1\]]ngan dang /_smre sngags 'don pa dang /_sdug bsngal ba dang /_yid mi bde ba rnams las yongs su grol zhing sdug bsngal las yongs su grol ba'o zhes smra ste/_de bas na des ni gang 'di skad du/_'dir ni zla phyed tshes brgyad dang /_/de bzhin bcu bzhi bco
[\[23a.2\]]lnga dang /_/cho 'phrul gyi ni zla phyed la'ang /_/gso sbyong yan lag brgyad pa la/_/shin tu mnyam gzhag gnas byed 'dir/_/nga ci 'dra bar de bzhin 'gyur/_/zhes tshigs su bcad pa 'di smras na legs par smras pa yin te/_nyes par smras pa ma yin no/_/legs par bstod
[\[23a.3\]]pa yin te nyes par bstod pa ma yin no/_/legs par brjod pa yin te nyes par brjod pa ma yin no zhes gsungs so/_/'dzam bu'i gling gi kho ra khor yug na/_'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po'i lam dpag tshad gcig tu gser gyi bye ma bdal te/_rgya mtsho chen po'i chus pus
[\[23a.4\]]mo nub pa tsam du yongs su khyab po/_/gang gi tshe 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po 'jig rten du 'byung ba'i tshe rgya mtsho chen po dpag tshad gnyis kyi bar du chu skam zhing med par 'gyur te/_'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po gang nas gling du 'gro ba de ni 'khor los sgyur ba'i lam yin no/_/bcom
[\[23a.5\]]ldan 'das kyis kyang 'di skad du/_dge slong dag sngon byung ba 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal pos glang po rin po che brtag par 'dod pas nyi ma shar ba'i dus kyi tshe glang po rin po che la zhon nas sa chen po rgya mtsho la thug pa 'di nyid bskor te/_rgyal po'i pho brang nas 'khor de nyid du song nas
[\[23a.6\]]khye'u sus kyi bya ba byed do/_/dge slong dag gzhan yang 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal pos rta rin po che brtag par 'dod pas nyi ma shar ba'i dus kyi tshe rta rin po che la zhon nas sa chen po rgya mtsho la thug pa 'di nyid bskor te/_rgyal po'i pho brang 'khor de nyid du song nas khye'u sus kyi bya ba byed do/_/_
[\[23a.7\]]zhes gsungs so/_/bsdus pa'i mdo la/_ri dang skye gnas dag dang ni/_/nam mkha' lding dang nyo tshong dang /_/grang ba dag ni lnga par byas/_/dus tshigs kyang ni tha ma yin/_/'jig rten gzhag pa las tshigs drug pa'o/_/mdo la/_/srung ma lha'i grong khyer srang rnams rgyal
[\[23b\]]
[\[23b.1\]]byed pa/_/chos bzangs rgyu ba'i lam dang 'obs dang skyed mos tshal/_/sa gzhi dang ni yongs 'du rdo dang glang chen rnams/_/lha ma yin rnams kyi yang de dang 'dra ba yin/_/lha'i grong khyer dang lha ma yin gyi grong gi bar du sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kyi srung ma rnam pa lnga bkod
[\[23b.2\]]pa la 'di lta ste/_chu na gnas pa'i klu rnams dang /_lag na gzhong thogs kyi lha rnams dang /_phreng thogs kyi lha rnams dang /_rtag tu myos kyi lha rnams dang /_rgyal po chen po bzhi rnams so/_/gang gi tshe lha ma yin rnams sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams dang /_lhan cig tu

[\[35b.2\]]gyi mtshams na sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kyi shing yongs 'du sa brtol zhes bya ba yod de/_yongs 'du las brtol gyi rtsa ba ni dpag tshad lnga bcu thur du zug go/_/'phang du ni dpag tshad brgya yod do/_/yal ga phyir gyes pa ni dpag tshad lnga bcu yod do/_/yongs 'du sa brtol gyi yal
[\[35b.3\]]ga lnga yod de/_yal ga gcig ni shar phyogs dpag tshad lnga bcur 'dud do/_/yal ga gnyis pa ni lho phyogs su dpag tshad lnga bcur 'dud do/_/yal ga gsum pa ni nub phyogs su dpag tshad lnga bcur 'dud do/_/yal ga bzhi pa ni byang phyogs su dpag tshad lnga bcur 'dud do/_/_

[\[35b.5\]]rdzi phyogs su ni dpag tshad brgyar ngad ldang ngo /_/rdzi phyogs ma yin par dpag tshad lnga bcur ngad ldang ngo /_/dpag tshad brgyad cur ni 'od dang kha dog gis lham me lhan ne lhang nger 'dug go/_/sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kyi shing yongs 'du sa brtol gyi lo ma ser ba na de'i tshe sum
[\[35b.6\]]cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kye ma/_yongs 'du sa brtol 'di lo ma ser ba las na da ni ring po mi thogs par 'dab ma lhags par 'gyur ro zhes nas kun tu dga' zhing rab tu dga' bas gnas pa gang yin pa de'i dus kyang yod la/_de'i skabs kyang yod do/_/sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha
[\[35b.7\]]rnams kyi shing yongs 'du sa brtol gyi 'dab ma lhags pa na de'i tshe sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kye ma yongs 'du sa brtol 'di 'dab ma lhags pa las na ring po mi thogs par sbal mig 'thon par 'gyur ro zhes nas kun tu dga' zhing rab tu dga' bas gnas pa gang yin pa de'i
[\[36a\]]
[\[36a.1\]]dus kyang yod la de'i skabs kyang yod do/_/sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kyi shing yongs 'du sa brtol sbal mig 'thon pa na de'i tshe sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kye ma yongs 'du sa brtol 'di sbal mig 'thon pa las na da ni ring por mi

[\[36a.3\]]ma yongs 'du sa brtol 'di sbal mig bye ba las na da ni ring po mi thogs par me tog kha 'bu bar 'gyur ro zhes nas kun tu dga' zhing rab tu dga' bas gnas pa gang yang yin pa de'i dus kyang yod la de'i skabs kyang yod do/_/sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kyi shing yongs

[\[36b\]]
[\[36b.1\]]sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kyi shing yongs 'du sa brtol gyi rtsa ba ni dpag tshad lnga bcur thur du zug go/_/'phang du ni dpag tshad brgyad yod do/_/yal ga dang /_lo ma dang /_yan lag rnams ni dpag tshad lnga bcur gyes so/_/dge slong dag sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kyi
[\[36b.2\]]shing yongs 'du sa brtol gyi lo ma ser ba na de'i tshe sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kye ma yongs 'du sa brtol 'di lo ma ser ba las na da ni ring po mi thogs par 'dab ma lhags par 'gyur ro zhes nas kun du dga' zhing rab tu dga' bas gnas pa gang yin pa de'i dus kyang yod do/_/_
[\[36b.3\]]dge slong dag sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kyi shing yongs 'du sa brtol gyi 'dab ma lhags pa na de'i tshe sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kye ma yongs 'du sa brtol 'di 'dab ma lhags pa las na da ni ring po mi thogs par sbal mig 'thon par 'gyur ro zhes nas kun nas dga' zhing rab tu
[\[36b.4\]]dga' bas gnas pa gang yin pas de'i dus kyang yod do/_/dge slong dag sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kyi shing yongs 'du sa brtol sbal mig 'thon pa de'i tshe sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kye ma yongs 'du sa brtol 'di sbal mig 'thon pa las na da ni ring po mi thogs par sbal

[\[41b.1\]]las grub pa ste/_gser gyi ra bas kun nas bskor ro/_/ra ba de'i 'phang du yang dpag tshad phyed do/_/ra ba de la rtsig skyabs 'di lta ste/_gser las byas pa dang /_dngul las byas pa dang /_bai DUr+ya las byas pa dang /_shel las byas pa rnam pa bzhi dang /_gyen du 'phang

[\[44a.1\]]dang /_bai DUr+ya las byas pa dang /_shel las byas pa rnam pa bzhi dang /_mda' yab dang /_ltad mo lta ba'i sa rnam pa bzhi yod do/_/de'i nang gis gzhi yang dbyibs legs shing blta na sdug la mdzes par bris shing legs par bris pa tshon sna brgya rtsa gcig

[\[44b.1\]]dang /_skad yid du 'ong ba dang /_skad snyan pa dang /_'dod dgur sgyur ba'i gzugs can rnams skad snyan pa 'byin to/_/de dag gi nye 'khor na me tog gi shing dang 'bras bu'i shing sna tshogs yod pa rnams legs par skyes shing dbyibs legs pa yongs su grub pa ste/_me tog phreng bar

[\[45a.1\]]pa dag kyang yod/_mer 'du shes pa dag kyang yod/_rlung du 'du shes pa dag kyang yod do/_/sems can me la sar 'du shes pa dag kyang yod/_chur 'du shes pa dag kyang yod/_mer 'du shes pa dag kyang yod/_rlung du 'du shes pa dag kyang yod do/_/sems

[\[45a.3\]]'du shes pa dag kyang yod do/_/sems can sa la bdag tu 'du shes pa dag kyang yod de/_sa'i khams gang yin pa de ni bdag yin la/_bdag gang yin pa de ni sa yin te/_de ltar sa dang bdag gnyis su dbyer med cing tha dad pa ma yin te/_bdag gi bdag ni rdzogs pa yin no zhes
[\[45a.4\]]nas de dag sa la bkur stir byed/_btsun par byed/_ri mor byed/_mchod par byed do/_/de dag gis bkur stir byas/_btsun par byas/_ri mor byas so/_/mchod par byas nas/_dga' zhing mgu la yi rangs te/_bkur stir byed cing nye bar brten te/_gnas la sems kyis lung
[\[45a.5\]]bstan pa yin no/_/sems can chu dang me dang rlung la bdag tu 'du shes pa dag kyang yod de/_rlung gang yin pa de ni bdag yin la/_bdag gang yin pa de ni rlung yin te/_de ltar rlung dang bdag gnyis su dbyer med cing tha dad pa ma yin te/_bdag gis bdag ni rdzogs pa yin no zhes nas

[\[45a.7\]]yin no/_/sems can sa la nam mkhar 'du shes pa dag kyang yod do/_/nam mkha' la sar 'du shes pa ji ltar bu zhe na/_/sa la nam mkhar 'du shes pa ji ltar bu zhe na/_til rmed pa'i mi la la zhig gis khron pa brko ba'i mi 'ga' zhig la 'di skad du/_kye sdong po me reg ma dang 'dra
[\[45b\]]
[\[45b.1\]]ba'i mi glang mthong ngam zhes smras so/_/des smras pa/_ma mthong ngo /_/til za'am mi za/_smras pa mi za'o zhes so/_/de ltar na sa la nam mkhar 'du shes pa yin no/_/ji ltar na nam mkha' la sar 'du shes she na/_smras pa/_ji ltar bram ze la la zhig bong bu'i shing rtas song
[\[45b.2\]]nas bong bu'i shing rta las babs te/_bong bu'i shing rta phur bu la btags nas phur bu nam mkha' la btab te/_btsugs nas mgo la bas dkris te/_sa la gan rkyal du nyal ba de bzhin du nam mkha' la sar 'du shes pa yin no/_/lo gcig la dus gcig tu mtshan mo ni yud
[\[45b.3\]]tsam bco brgyad/_nyin mo ni yud tsam bcu gnyis yod do/_/lo gcig la dus gcig tu mtshan mo ni yud tsam bco brgyad/_nyin mo ni yud tsam bcu gnyis pa de gang zhe na/_dgun zla tha chungs yar gyi ngo tshes brgyad la mtshan mo ni yud tsam bco brgyad/_nyin mo ni yud tsam

[\[54b.1\]]dang /_bzhi dang /_gsum dang /_gnyis dang /_gcig lus par 'gyur zhing /_nyi ma lnga pa 'jig rten du byung bas rgya mtsho chen po'i chu tA la bdun tsam lus par 'gyur zhing tA la drug dang /_lnga dang /_bzhi dang /_gsum dang /_gnyis dang /_gcig tsam lus par 'gyur ro/_/nyi ma lnga
