[\[95a.3\]]kyi tshad kyang de tsam ste/_dge slong dag 'di ni skyes bu chen po'i skyes bu chen po'i mtshan yin no/_/dge slong dag skyes bu chen po ni lus kyi spu gyen du phyogs pa dang /_dge slong dag skyes bu chen po ni spu re re nas skye ba ste/_lus kyi spu rnams re re nas skye zhing 'jam la reg na bde ba
[\[95a.4\]]dang /_mthon mthing du 'dug pa dang /_'khyil ba dang /_g.yas phyogs su 'khyil ba ste/_dge slong dag 'di ni skyes bu chen po'i skyes bu chen po'i mtshan yin no/_/dge slong dag skyes bu chen po'i lus kyi pags pa gser 'dra bas na gser gyi mdog can yin te/_dge slong
[\[95a.5\]]dag 'di ni skyes bu chen po'i skyes bu chen po'i mtshan yin no/_/dge slong dag skyes bu chen po ni 'od 'dom gang dang ldan te/_dge slong dag 'di ni skyes bu chen po'i skyes bu chen po'i mtshan yin no/_/dge slong dag skyes bu chen po ni lus kyi pags pa srab pa ste/_pags pa
[\[95a.6\]]srab pas na lus la rdul dang dri mas mi chags te/_dge slong dag 'di ni skyes bu chen po'i skyes bu chen po'i mtshan yin no/_/dge slong dag skyes bu chen po ni bdun shin tu mtho ba ste/_lus kyi bdun mtho bar gyur pa ni lag pa gnyis dang /_rkang pa gnyis dang /_thal
[\[95a.7\]]gong gnyis dang /_ltag pa ste/_dge slong dag 'di ni skyes bu chen po'i skyes bu chen po'i mtshan yin no/_/dge slong dag skyes bu chen po ni thal gong rgyas pa ste/_dge slong dag 'di ni skyes bu chen po'i skyes bu chen po'i mtshan yin no/_/dge slong dag skyes bu chen po ni
[\[95b\]]
[\[95b.1\]]ro stod seng ge 'dra ba ste/_dge slong dag 'di ni skyes bu chen po'i skyes bu chen po'i mtshan yin no/_/dge slong dag skyes bu chen po ni lus che zhing drang ba ste/_dge slong dag 'di ni skyes bu chen po'i skyes bu chen po'i mtshan yin no/_/dge slong dag skyes bu chen po ni dpung mgo shin tu
[\[95b.2\]]zlum pa ste/_dge slong dag 'di ni skyes bu chen po'i skyes bu chen po'i mtshan yin no/_/dge slong dag skyes bu chen po ni so bzhi bcu yod pa ste/_dge slong dag 'di ni skyes bu chen po'i skyes bu chen po'i mtshan yin no/_/dge slong dag skyes bu chen po ni so mnyam pa ste/_dge slong
[\[95b.3\]]dag 'di ni skyes bu chen po'i skyes bu chen po'i mtshan yin no/_/dge slong dag skyes bu chen po ni so thags bzang ba ste/_dge slong dag 'di ni skyes bu chen po'i skyes bu chen po'i mtshan yin no/_/dge slong dag skyes bu chen po ni mche ba shin tu dkar ba ste/_dge slong dag 'di ni
[\[95b.4\]]skyes bu chen po'i skyes bu chen po'i mtshan yin no/_/dge slong dag skyes bu chen po ni 'gram pa seng ge 'dra ba ste/_dge slong dag 'di ni skyes bu chen po'i skyes bu chen po'i mtshan yin no/_/dge slong dag skyes bu chen po ni ro bro ba'i mchog brnyes pa ste/_dge slong dag 'di ni
[\[95b.5\]]skyes bu chen po'i skyes bu chen po'i mtshan yin no/_/dge slong dag skyes bu chen po ni lce ring zhing srab pa ste/_lce ring zhing srab pas na kha nas phyung na lces skra'i mtshams su thug par kha thams cad khebs te/_dge slong dag 'di ni skyes bu chen po'i skyes bu chen po'i mtshan yin no/_/_
[\[95b.6\]]dge slong dag skyes bu chen po ni tshangs pa'i dbyangs bya ka la ping ka'i ltar sgra snyan cing rnga bo che'i sgra lta bu dang ldan pa ste/_dge slong dag 'di ni skyes bu chen po'i skyes bu chen po'i mtshan yin no/_/dge slong dag skyes bu chen po ni mig mthon mthing lta bu ste/_dge slong dag 'di ni
[\[95b.7\]]skyes bu chen po'i skyes bu chen po'i mtshan yin no/_/dge slong dag skyes bu chen po ni ba'i rdzi ma lta bu dang ldan te/_dge slong dag 'di ni skyes bu chen po'i skyes bu chen po'i mtshan yin no/_/dge slong dag skyes bu chen po ni mgo bo gtsug tor dang ldan pa ste/_dge slong dag 'di ni
[\[96a\]]
[\[96a.1\]]skyes bu chen po'i skyes bu chen po'i mtshan yin no/_/dge slong dag skyes bu chen po ni smin mtshams su mdzod spu skyes pa dkar zhing 'jam la reg na bde ba dang /_g.yas su 'khyil pa dang ldan te/_dge slong dag 'di ni skyes bu chen po'i skyes bu chen
[\[96a.2\]]po'i mtshan yin no/_/dge slong dag skyes bu chen po'i mtshan sum cu rtsa gnyis ni de dag yin te/_skyes bu chen po'i mtshan de dag dang ldan na rnam pa gnyis su 'gyur gyi gzhan du mi 'gyur te/_gal te khyim par 'dug cing khyim na gnas na ni 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po mtha'
[\[96a.3\]]bzhir rgyal ba chos kyi rgyal po chos dang ldan pa rin po che sna bdun dang ldan par 'gyur ro/_/de'i rin po che sna bdun ni 'di lta bu yin te/_'di lta ste/_'khor lo rin po che dang /_glang po rin po che dang /_rta rin po che dang /_nor bu rin po che dang /_bud med rin po che dang /_khyim bdag
[\[96a.4\]]rin po che dang /_bdun pa ste/_blon po rin po che'o/_/de'i bu ni stong tham pa yod de/_dpa' ba rtul phod pa yan lag mchog gi gzugs dang ldan pa pha rol gyi sde rab tu 'joms pa sha stag go/_/de ni rgya mtsho la thug pa'i sa chen po ma lus pa gnod par sdo ba med cing 'tshe ba med
[\[96a.5\]]pa 'di nyid chad pa med cing mtshon gyis bda' ba med la chos dang mthun zhing snyoms pas legs par phab ste gnas so/_/gal te skra dang kha spu rnams bregs te gos ngur smrig dag bgos nas/_dad pas khyim nas khyim med par legs pa kho nar rab tu byung na ni 'jig rten
[\[96a.6\]]'dir de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas su 'gyur te/_rgya cher grags par 'gyur ro/_/bcom ldan 'das kyis de skad ces bka' stsal te/_bde bar gshegs pas de skad gsungs nas/_ston pas gzhan yang 'di skad ces
[\[96a.7\]]bka' stsal to/_/thub chen bdag nyid rab bsgoms pa/_/lus kyi tha ma 'dzin pa yi/_/lus kyi mtshan rnams yod pa dag_/nga yis rab tu bshad par bya/_/de yi rkang pa shin tu gnas/_/sa la mnyam par gnon pa yin/_/de yi rkang gnyis 'og mthil na/_/'khor lo
[\[96b\]]
[\[96b.1\]]rab tu dbyibs legs yod/_/lag sor yang ni ring ba ste/_/rkang pa rting pa yangs par ldan/_/lag dang rkang pa dra bar 'brel/_/shing bal lta bur 'jam pa yin/_/de yi long mo'i tshigs mi mngon/_/mi mchog rje ngar e ne ya/_/lus ni thur du ma btud par/_/lag
[\[96b.2\]]gis pus mo'i lha ngar slebs/_/mdoms kyi sba ba sbubs su nub/_/n+ya gro d+ha ltar chu zheng gab/_/lus spu rnams ni gyen du phyogs/_/de spu g.yas phyogs re re 'khyil/_/gser gyi kha dog 'dra ba dang /_/'dom gang 'od ni kun nas 'khor/_/lus kyi pags pa srab
[\[96b.3\]]pa dang /_/de yi bdun po mtho ba yin/_/sgrog rus dag kyang sha yis gang /_/ro stod seng ge 'dra ba yin/_/lus ni che zhing drang ba dang /_/de yi phrag pa dbyibs kyang legs/_/so ni bzhi bcu yod pa ste/_/yongs su tshang zhing nyams pa med/_/mnyam zhing thags kyang
[\[96b.4\]]bzang ba ste/_/de yi so rnams dbyibs kyang legs/_/mche ba rab dkar seng ge'i 'gram/_/ro rnams bro ba'i mchog rnyed pa/_/lce ni ring zhing srab pa ste/_/tshangs pa'i dbyangs dang ldan pa yin/_/mig ni mthin mthong ba rdzi ma/_/de yi mgo ni gtsug tor ldan/_/_
[\[96b.5\]]de ni smin mtshams mdzod spu yod/_/dung ltar dkar zhing mdzes pa yin/_/thub chen bdag nyid rab bsgoms pa/_/lus kyi tha ma 'dzin pa yi/_/lus la mtshan rnams yod pa ni/_/sum cu rtsa gnyis de dag yin/_/gang gi lus la mtshan rtags rnams/_/sum cu rtsa
[\[96b.6\]]gnyis ldan gyur pa/_/de lta bu ni rgyal gyur nas/_/sa yi steng ni 'dul bar byed/_/yang na byang chub mchog kyang 'thob/_/dran dang ldan zhing bu mang la/_/nad med shin tu mkhas par 'gyur/_/zas dang skom dang bgo ba dang /_/mal cha stan rnams rnyed par 'gyur/_/_
[\[96b.7\]]de ni mi phyed 'khor dang ldan/_/lus can kun gyi yid du 'ong /_/de lta bu ni lha mi rnams/_/rjes su mthun par byed par 'gyur/_/de lta bu yi mi dag ni/_/chos kyi dbang gis mchog yin no/_/mi mnyam pa dang zla med dang /_/mtshungs med rnam par 'dren par 'gyur/_/bcom
[\[97a\]]
[\[97a.1\]]ldan 'das kyis de skad ces bka' stsal nas/_dge slong de dag yi rangs te/_bcom ldan 'das kyis gsungs pa la mngon par bstod do/_/ci'i phyir byang chub sems dpa' skyes bu chen po'i mtshan rkang pa shin tu gnas pa thob ce na/_
[\[97a.2\]]smras pa/_byang chub sems dpas ni sngon gyi srid pa dang /_sngon gyi gnas dang /_sngon gyi lus dang /_sngon gyi bdag nyid thob pa dang /_sngon gyi tshe rabs gzhan dag dang /_'das pa dang /_zad pa dang /_'gags pa dang /_bral ba dang /_rnam par gyur pa dang /_yongs
[\[97a.3\]]su zad pa dag tu dge ba'i chos 'di lta ste/_bden pa'am/_tshul khrims sam/_gtong ba'am/_brtul zhugs sam/_yi dam gang dang gang yang dag par blangs te gnas par gyur kyang rung ste/_de tshul khrims dang /_brtul zhugs dang /_yi dam de la yi dam
[\[97a.4\]]dam por gyur cing yi dam brtan por gyur to/_/yi dam brten por gyur nas kyang mi g.yo kun nas mi g.yo/_kun tu rab tu mi g.yo'o/_/mi 'gul/_kun tu mi 'gul kun tu rab tu mi 'gul lo/_/mi 'khrugs/_kun tu mi 'khrugs/_kun tu rab tu mi 'khrugs
[\[97a.5\]]so/_/mi 'phrogs/_kun tu mi 'phrogs/_kun tu rab tu mi 'phrogs te/_de las de dang /_yang dag par blangs pa de lta bu dang /_yang dag par bzung ba de lta bus lus zhig nas dga' ldan gyi lha rnams dang skal ba mnyam par skye'o/_/de der skyes nas ring po ma
[\[97a.6\]]lon par dga' ldan gyi ris kyi lha sngar skyes pa rnams las lha'i gnas gsum gyis 'phags te/_gsum gang zhe na/_'di lta ste/_lha'i tshe dang /_lha'i kha dog dang /_lha'i grags pas 'phags so/_/de der tshe'i tshad ji tsam pa de srid du gnas nas de nas shi 'phos nas khams 'dir
[\[97a.7\]]mi rnams dang skal ba mnyam par skye'o/_/de 'dir rgyal po'i pho brang ngam/_mdun na 'don gyi khyim du skye bar 'gyur te/_der byang chub sems dpa' des skyes bu chen po'i mtshan rkang pa shin tu gnas pa rnyed par 'gyur ro/_/de'i snga ltas ni 'di yin te/_gal te khyim par
[\[97b\]]
[\[97b.1\]]'dug cing khyim na gnas na ni 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po mtha' bzhir rgyal ba chos kyi rgyal po chos dang ldan pa/_rin po che sna bdun dang ldan par 'gyur ro/_/de'i rin po che sna bdun ni 'di lta bu yin te/_'di lta ste/_'khor lo rin po che nas bdun pa ste/_blon po rin po
[\[97b.2\]]che'i bar rnams so/_/de'i bu ni stong tham pa yod de/_dpa' ba rtul phod pa yan lag mchog gi gzugs dang ldan pa/_pha rol gyi sde rab tu 'joms pa sha stag go/_/de ni rgya mtsho la thug pa'i sa chen po ma lus pa gnod par sdo ba med cing 'tshe ba med pa 'di nyid chad pa med
[\[97b.3\]]cing mtshon gyis bda' ba med la chos dang mthun shing snyoms pas legs par phab ste gnas la/_rgyal srid de las dgra 'am/_phyir rgol ba'am/_rgyal po do zla'am/_sa'i bdag po'am/_rgyal rigs kyis mi g.yo/_kun tu mi g.yo/_kun tu rab tu mi g.yo'o/_/mi
[\[97b.4\]]'gul/_kun tu mi 'gul/_kun tu rab tu mi 'gul lo/_/mi 'khrugs/_kun tu mi 'khrugs/_kun tu rab tu mi 'khrugs so/_/mi 'phrogs/_kun tu mi 'phrogs/_kun tu rab tu mi 'phrogs so/_/btsun mo'i 'khor dang /_gzhon nu rnams dang /_blon po rnams
[\[97b.5\]]dang /_gtso bo dang /_dmag gi ru dang /_grong mi dang /_yul mi rnams kyis bkur stir byed/_bla mar byed/_ri mor byed/_mchod par byed do/_/gal te skra dang kha spu rnams bregs te gos ngur smrig dag bgos nas/_dad pas khyim nas khyim med pa legs pa kho nar rab
[\[97b.6\]]tu byung na ni 'jig rten du de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas su 'gyur te/_sgra cher grags par 'gyur ro zhes gsungs te/_de dge slong gi tshul des dge sbyong ngam/_bram ze'am/_lha 'am/_bdud dam/_tshangs pa'am/_gzhan
[\[97b.7\]]su yang rung bas chos dang mthun pas mi g.yo/_kun tu mi g.yo/_kun tu rab tu mi g.yo'o/_/mi 'gul/_kun tu mi 'gul/_kun tu rab tu mi 'gul lo/_/mi 'khrugs/_kun tu mi 'khrugs/_kun tu rab tu mi 'khrugs so/_/mi 'phrogs/_kun tu mi 'phrogs/_
[\[98a\]]
[\[98a.1\]]kun tu rab tu mi 'phrogs so/_/dge slong rnams dang /_dge slong ma rnams dang /_dge bsnyen rnams dang /_dge bsnyen ma rnams dang /_lha rnams dang /_klu rnams dang /_lha ma yin rnams dang /_nam mkha' lding rnams dang /_dri za rnams
[\[98a.2\]]dang /_mi'am ci rnams dang /_lto 'phye chen po rnams dang /_gnod sbyin rnams dang /_srin po rnams dang /_mi rnams dang /_mi ma yin pa rnams kyis bkur stir byed/_bla mar byed/_ri mor byed/_mchod par byed de/_'di ni de'i snga ltas yin no/_/'di la chos nyid ni 'di
[\[98a.3\]]yin te/_de la 'di skad ces bya'o/_/gang tshe bde gshegs zhabs ni shin tu gnas pa yi/_/mtshan ni gang gis brnyes gyur de dag mnyan par gyis/_/bde ba dang ni tshul khrims brtul zhugs gtong ba dang /_/chos dge bde ba skyed pa gzhan rnams gang yin pa/_/_
[\[98a.4\]]nyid kyis yang dag blangs te brtan por gnas gyur des/_/gom pa brtan por lhun po bzhin du g.yo ba med/_/ci'i phyir byang chub sems dpas skyes bu chen po'i mtshan rkang pa gnyis kyi 'og mthil nas 'khor lo skye ba thob ce na/_smras pa/_byang chub sems dpas ni sngon
[\[98a.5\]]gyi srid pa zhes bya ba nas/_rgyas par sngon gyi skye ba gzhan dag gi bar dang /_'das pa dang /_zad pa dang /_'gags pa dang /_bral ba dang /_rnam par gyur pa dang /_yongs su zad pa dag tu pha ma dang /_nye du dang /_rgan rabs dang /_bla ma lta bu rnams dang /_gzhan
[\[98a.6\]]dge sbyong dang /_bram ze gnod par bya ba ma yin pa rnams dang /_gnod par bya ba la mi dga' ba gang yin pa de dag dang /_tha na bya dang /_ri dgas yan chad la yang chos dang mthun par bsrung ba dang /_bskyab pa dang /_sba ba byas la/_de nas snying brtse ba can gyi tshul khrims
[\[98a.7\]]kyang yang dag par blangs te gnas par gyur to/_/de las de dang /_yang dag par blangs pa de lta bu dang /_yang dag par bzung ba de lta bus lus zhig nas dga' ldan gyi lha rnams dang skal ba mnyam par skye'o/_/de der skyes nas ring po ma lon par dga' ldan gyi ris kyi lha sngar
[\[98b\]]
[\[98b.1\]]skyes pa rnams las lha'i gnas gsum gyis 'phags te zhes bya ba nas rgyas par sbyar te/_de de nas shi 'phos nas khams 'dir mi rnams dang skal ba mnyam par skye'o zhes bya ba'i bar du sbyar ro/_/de 'dir rgyal po'i pho brang ngam/_mdun na 'don gyi khyim du skye bar 'gyur te/_/_
[\[98b.2\]]der byang chub sems dpa' des skyes bu chen po'i mtshan rkang pa gnyis kyi 'og gi mthil 'khor lo 'byung ba thob par 'gyur ro/_/de'i snga ltas ni 'di yin te/_gal te khyim par 'dug cing khyim na gnas na ni 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po mtha' bzhir rgyal ba zhes bya ba nas/_
[\[98b.3\]]rgyas par chos dang mthun zhing snyoms pas legs par phab ste gnas so zhes bya ba'i bar du sbyar te/_lha'i 'khor lo rin po che thob par 'gyur la/_de nas gling bzhi legs par phab te gling bzhir rgyal srid kyi dbang phyug la dbang byed do/_/btsun mo'i 'khor dang /_gzhon
[\[98b.4\]]nu rnams zhes bya ba nas rgyas par ri mor byed/_mchod par byed ces bya ba'i bar du sbyar ro/_/gal te skra dang /_kha spu rnams bregs te zhes bya ba nas/_rab tu byung na ni/_'jig rten du de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas su 'gyur te/_
[\[98b.5\]]sgra cher grags par 'gyur ba'i bar du gsungs te/_'phags pa'i lam yan lag brgyad pa brnyes par gyur la/_des na nyon mongs pa thams cad spangs nas chos thams cad la sgrib pa med pa'i ye shes brnyes par gyur te/_dge slong rnams dang /_dge slong ma rnams zhes bya ba
[\[98b.6\]]nas rgyas par ri mor byed/_mchod par byed ces bya ba'i bar du sbyar te/_'di ni de'i snga ltas yin no/_/'di la chos nyid ni 'di yin te/_de la 'di skad ces bya'o/_/pha ma dang ni gnyen rnams dang /_/de bzhin gzhan yang bla ma gang /_/ri dgas bya rnams de bzhin te/_/chos dang mthun pas bsrung byas
[\[98b.7\]]pa/_/dge ba de yi rnam smin gyis/_/rtsibs stong bcas dang lte bar bcas/_/mu khyud bcas pa'i 'khor lo dag_/rkang pa gnyis kyi mthil du byung /_/ci'i phyir byang chub sems dpas skyes bu chen po'i mtshan sor mo ring ba dang /_rkang pa'i rting pa yangs pa dang /_lus che
[\[99a\]]
[\[99a.1\]]zhing drang ba gsum thob ce na/_smras pa/_byang chub sems dpas ni/_sngon gyi srid pa zhes bya ba nas rgyas par sbyar te/_srog chags 'byung ba sems can thams cad tha na srog chags grog spur yan chad kyi phyir srog gcod pa spangs te/_srog
[\[99a.2\]]gcod pa las phyir log nas/_dbyug pa spangs shing mtshon cha spangs ste ngo tsha shes shing snying rje dang ldan pas srog gcod pa spangs pa dang /_gzhan yang byang chub sems dpas ma byin par len pa spangs te ma byin par len pa las phyir log nas/_byin pa len pa dang /_byin
[\[99a.3\]]pa la dga' ba dang /_byin pa dang /_btang ba dang /_bor ba 'dod pa dang /_mi rku ba dang /_gtsang mar gyur pa dang /_dag pa dang /_gtsang mas bdag nyid bsrungs te/_ma byin par len pa spangs nas ma byin par len pa las sems yongs su dag par byas par gyur pa
[\[99a.4\]]dang /_gzhan yang byang chub sems dpas pha ma dang /_nye du dang /_rgan rabs dang /_bla ma lta bu rnams dang /_gzhan yang dge sbyong dang /_bram ze kha na ma tho ba med pa dang /_kha na ma tho ba med pa la dga' ba gang yin pa de dag la gsong por smra ba dang /_phyag 'tshal ba
[\[99a.5\]]dang /_langs te stan stobs par byed de/_de las de dang yang dag par blangs pa de lta bu dang /_yang dag par bzung ba de lta bus lus zhig nas dga' ldan gyi lha rnams dang skal ba mnyam par skye'o/_/de der skyes nas ring po ma lon par dga' ldan gyi ris kyi lha sngar skyes
[\[99a.6\]]pa rnams las lha'i gnas gsum gyis 'phags te zhes bya ba nas rgyas par sbyar te/_de de nas shi 'phos nas khams 'dir mi rnams dang skal ba mnyam par skye'o zhes bya ba'i bar du sbyar ro/_/de 'dir rgyal po'i pho brang ngam/_mdun na 'don gyi khyim du skye bar 'gyur te/_
[\[99a.7\]]der byang chub sems dpa' des/_skyes bu chen po'i mtshan sor mo ring ba dang /_rkang pa'i rting pa yangs pa dang /_lus che zhing drang ba thob par 'gyur ro/_/de'i snga ltas ni 'di yin te/_gal te khyim par 'dug cing khyim na gnas na ni 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po mtha' bzhir
[\[99b\]]
[\[99b.1\]]rgyal ba zhes bya ba nas rgyas par sbyar te/_tshe ring zhing yun ring du gnas par 'gyur ba dang /_bkur stir byed/_bla mar byed/_ri mor byed/_mchod par byed ces bya ba'i bar du rgyas par sbyar ro/_/gal te skra dang /_kha spu bregs te zhes bya ba nas/_rab tu byung na ni 'jig
[\[99b.2\]]rten du de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas su 'gyur te/_sgra cher grags par 'gyur ro zhes bya ba'i bar du gsungs te/_bcom ldan 'das kyis bzhed na bskal pa 'am/_bskal pa las lhag par yang sku tshe ring zhing yun ring du
[\[99b.3\]]gnas par 'gyur ba dang /_bkur stir byed/_bla mar byed ces bya ba'i bar du rgyas par sbyar te/_'di ni de'i snga ltas yin no/_/'di la chos nyid ni 'di yin te/_de la 'di skad ces bya'o/_/gang tshe rgyal ba sor mo ring bar gyur pa dang /_/zhabs kyi rting yangs sku che
[\[99b.4\]]drang bar gyur pa ni/_/srog chags srog gcod pa las slar ni log gyur dang /_/ma byin pa dang rku ba spangs par gyur pa dang /_/dge sbyong bram ze rnams la gsong bor smra ba dang /_/des ni bla ma rnams la ldang zhing stan byin pa'i/_/las dge bde ba skyed pa rnam
[\[99b.5\]]smin dge ba de/_/skye ba gzhan dag tu ni ston pa mdzad pa'i phyir/_/ston pa de la las kyi rnam smin de 'dra ba'i/_/mtshan rnams sku las byung ste gsum dang gsum du sbyar/_/ci'i phyir byang chub sems dpas skyes bu chen po'i mtshan lag pa dang rkang pa dra ba dang ldan
[\[99b.6\]]pa thob ce na/_smras pa/_byang chub sems dpas ni sngon gyi srid pa zhes bya ba nas rgyas par sbyar te/_bsdu ba'i dngos po bzhis 'khor bsdus te/_'di lta ste/_sbyin pa dang /_snyan par smra ba dang /_don spyod pa dang /_don mthun pas so/_/de las de dang yang dag
[\[99b.7\]]par blangs pa de lta bu dang /_yang dag par gzung ba de lta bus lus zhig nas dga' ldan gyi lha rnams dang skal ba mnyam par skye'o zhes bya ba nas rgyas par sbyar te/_de de nas shi 'phos nas khams 'dir mi rnams dang skal ba mnyam bar skye'o zhes bya ba'i bar du sbyar ro/_/_
[\[100a\]]
[\[100a.1\]]de 'dir rgyal po'i pho brang ngam/_mdun na 'don gyi khyim du skye bar 'gyur te/_der byang chub sems dpa' des/_skyes bu chen po'i mtshan lag pa dang rkang pa dra ba dang ldan pa thob par 'gyur ro/_/de'i snga ltas ni 'di yin te/_gal te khyim bar
[\[100a.2\]]'dug cing khyim na gnas na ni 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po mtha' bzhir rgyal ba zhes bya ba nas rgyas par sbyar te/_btsun mo'i 'khor dang /_gzhon nu rnams dang /_blon po rnams dang /_gtso bo dang /_dmag gi ru dang /_grong mi dang /_yul gyi mi rnams
[\[100a.3\]]kyis bsten pa dang /_bkur sti byed pa nas rgyas par sbyar ro/_/gal te skra dang kha spu rnams bregs te gos ngur smrig dag bgos nas/_dad pas khyim nas khyim med par legs pa kho nar rab tu byung na ni 'jig rten du de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag
[\[100a.4\]]par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas su 'gyur te/_sgra cher grags par 'gyur ro zhes gsungs te/_dge slong rnams dang /_dge slong ma rnams dang /_dge bsnyen rnams dang /_dge bsnyen ma rnams dang /_gzhan mu stegs can dang /_dge sbyong dang /_bram ze dang /_
[\[100a.5\]]spyod pa pa dang /_kun tu rgyu rnams kyis bsten pa dang /_bkur sti byed/_bla mar byed ces bya ba nas rgyas par sbyar te/_'di ni de'i snga ltas yin no/_/'di la chos nyid ni 'di yin te/_de la 'di skad ces bya'o/_/gang gi lag pa rkang pa la/_/dra bar ldan pa yongs
[\[100a.6\]]rdzogs pa/_/ngang pa'i rgyal po ji lta bar/_/skyes bu mchog kyang de dang 'dra/_/'dir ni sems can rnams la yang /_/sbyin dang snyan par smra ba dang /_/don spyod dang ni don mthun pa/_/de dang de la ci rigs par/_/bsdu ba'i dngos po bzhi rnams kyis/_/sngon gyis bsdus
[\[100a.7\]]par gyur pas na/_/las kyi rnam par smin pa des/_/lag dang rkang pa dra bar ldan/_/ci'i phyir byang chub sems dpas skyes bu chen po'i mtshan lag pa dang rkang pa 'jam zhing gzhon sha chags pa thob ce na/_smras pa/_byang chub sems dpas ni sngon gyi srid pa zhes bya
[\[100b\]]
[\[100b.1\]]ba nas rgyas par sbyar te/_pha ma dang /_nye du dang /_rgan rabs dang /_bla ma lta bu rnams dang /_gzhan yang dge sbyong dang /_bram ze gnod par bya ba ma yin pa dang /_gnod par bya ba la mi dga' ba gang yin pa de dag la lus bsku zhing dril ba dang /_khrus bya ba dang /_
[\[100b.2\]]mar dang /_til mar rnams kyis dad pa'i sems kyis rang gi lag gis byi dor byas te/_de las de dang yang dag par blangs pa de lta bu dang /_yang dag par bzung ba de lta bus lus zhig nas dga' ldan gyi lha rnams dang skal ba mnyam par skye'o zhes bya ba nas rgyas par sbyar te/_
[\[100b.3\]]de de nas shi 'phos nas khams 'dir mi rnams dang skal ba mnyam par skye'o zhes bya ba nas rgyas par sbyar ro/_/der byang chub sems dpa' des skyes bu chen po'i mtshan lag pa dang rkang pa 'jam zhing gzhon sha chags pa thob par 'gyur ro/_/de'i snga ltas ni 'di yin te/_
[\[100b.4\]]gal te khyim par 'dug cing khyim na gnas na ni 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po mtha' bzhir rgyal ba zhes bya ba nas rgyas par sbyar te/_lus bsku zhing dril ba dang /_khrus bya ba dang /_mar dang til mar rnyed ces bya ba dang /_bkur sti byed/_bla mar byed ces bya ba nas
[\[100b.5\]]rgyas par sbyar ro/_/gal te skra dang kha spu rnams bregs te gos ngur smrig dag bgos nas/_dad pas khyim nas khyim med par legs pa kho nar rab tu byung na ni 'jig rten du de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas su 'gyur te/_sgra cher
[\[100b.6\]]grags par 'gyur ro zhes gsungs te/_lus bsku zhing dril ba dang /_khrus bya ba dang /_mar dang /_til mar rnams rnyed ces bya ba dang /_bkur sti byed/_bla mar byed ces bya ba nas rgyas par sbyar te/_'di ni de'i snga ltas yin no/_/'di la chos nyid ni 'di yin te/_
[\[100b.7\]]de la 'di skad ces bya'o/_/shing bal gyi ni 'da' ba ltar/_/lag pa rkang pa 'jam pa dang /_/reg na bde bar 'gyur ba yi/_/mtshan de gang gis thob ce na/_/bsku zhing dril dang khrus byas gang /_/mar dang til mar sbyin pa dang /_/des na de yi rkang lag ni/_/'jam zhing
[\[101a\]]
[\[101a.1\]]reg na bde ba yin/_/ci'i phyir byang chub sems dpas skyes bu chen po'i mtshan rkang pa long mo'i tshigs mi mngon pa dang /_lus kyi sru gyen du phyogs pa gnyis thob ce na/_smras pa/_byang chub sems dpas ni sngon gyi srid pa zhes bya ba nas rgyas par
[\[101a.2\]]sbyar te/_dge ba'i chos 'di lta ste/_bde ba'am/_tshul khrims sam/_gtong ba'am/_brtul zhugs sam/_yi dam gang dang gang yang dag par blangs te gnas par gyur kyang rung ste/_de lan 'ga' yang dma' bas chog par mi 'dzin cing /_ches gong nas gong du
[\[101a.3\]]khyad par shin tu 'dod pas cher gnas te/_de las de dang /_yang dag par blangs pa de lta bu dang /_yang dag par bzung ba de lta bus lus zhig nas dga' ldan gyi lha rnams dang skal ba mnyam par skye'o/_/de nas shi 'phos nas khams 'dir ni mi rnams dang skal ba
[\[101a.4\]]mnyam par skye'o zhes bya ba nas rgyas par sbyar te/_der byang chub sems dpa' des skyes bu chen po'i mtshan rkang pa long mo'i tshigs mi mngon pa dang /_lus kyi spu gyen du phyogs pa gnyis thob par 'gyur ro/_/de'i snga ltas ni 'di yin te/_gal te khyim par 'dug
[\[101a.5\]]cing khyim na gnas na ni 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po mtha' bzhir rgyal ba zhes bya ba nas rgyas par sbyar te/_grong rnams dang /_grong khyer rnams dang /_ljongs rnams kyis 'phel bar 'gyur ba dang /_bkur sti byed/_bla mar byed ces bya ba nas rgyas par sbyar ro/_/_
[\[101a.6\]]gal te skra dang kha spu rnams bregs te zhes bya ba nas/_rab tu byung na ni 'jig rten du de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas su 'gyur te/_sgra cher grags par 'gyur ro zhes bya ba'i bar du gsungs so/_/nges par 'byung ba dang /_dben
[\[101a.7\]]pa las skyes pa'i dag ba'i chos rnams kyis 'phel ba dang /_bkur sti byed ces bya ba nas rgyas par sbyar te/_'di ni de'i snga ltas yin no/_/'di la chos nyid ni 'di yin te/_de la 'di skad ces bya'o/_/gang tshe bde gshegs zhabs kyi long mo'i tshigs mi mngon/_/_
[\[101b\]]
[\[101b.1\]]gang tshe de yi spu rnams gyen du phyogs gyur pa/_/bden pa dang ni tshul khrims brtul zhugs gtong ba dang /_/chos dge bde ba bskyed pa gzhan rnams gang yin pa/_/de dag gong nas gong du khyad par 'dod byed cing /_/bzang zhing dkar ba rnams kyis chog par mi 'dzin
[\[101b.2\]]pa/_/des na de ni der yang khyad par thob par 'gyur/_/de phyir de yi lus la mtshan ni rnam gnyis 'byung /_/ci'i phyir byang chub sems dpas skyes bu chen po'i mtshan rje ngar ri dgas e ne ya'i lta bu thob ce na/_smras pa/_byang chub sems dpas ni sngon gyi srid pa
[\[101b.3\]]zhes bya ba nas rgyas par sbyar te/_gus pas chos blangs pa dang /_gzung ba dang /_'dzin du bcug pa dang /_bklags pa dang /_gzhan yang byang chub sems dpas sems can skye ba'i chos can rnams kyi skye ba spong ba'i phyir chos ston pa dang /_sems can rga ba'i
[\[101b.4\]]chos can rnams dang /_na ba dang /_'chi ba dang /_mya ngan dang /_smre sngags 'don pa dang /_sdug bsngal ba dang /_yid mi bde ba dang /_'khrug pa'i chos can rnams kyi 'khrug pa spong ba'i phyir chos ston pa dang /_gzhan yang byang chub sems dpas pha ma dang /_
[\[101b.5\]]nye du dang /_rgan rabs dang /_bla ma lta bu rnams dang /_gzhan yang dge sbyong dang /_bram ze gnod par bya ba ma yin pa dang /_gnod par bya ba la mi dga' ba gang yin pa de dag gi chos dang mthun pa'i phrin rnams dus bzhin du bskyal te/_de las de dang yang dag
[\[101b.6\]]par blangs pa de lta bu dang /_yang dag par bzung ba de lta bus lus zhig nas dga' ldan gyi lha rnams dang skal ba mnyam par skye'o zhes bya ba nas rgyas par sbyar ro/_/de de nas shi 'phos nas khams 'dir mi rnams dang skal ba mnyam par skye'o zhes bya ba'i bar du rgyas par
[\[101b.7\]]sbyar te/_der byang chub sems dpa' des skyes bu chen po'i mtshan rje ngar ri dgas e ne ya'i lta bu thob par 'gyur ro/_/de'i snga ltas ni 'di yin te/_gal te khyim par 'dug cing khyim na gnas na ni 'khor bos sgyur ba'i rgyal po mtha' bzhir rgyal ba zhes bya ba nas
[\[102a\]]
[\[102a.1\]]rgyas par sbyar te/_dran pa dang ldan pa'i mchog dang /_/blo gros dang ldan pa'i mchog dang /_bkur sti byed/_bla mar byed ces bya ba nas rgyas par sbyar ro/_/gal te skra dang kha spu rnams bregs te zhes bya ba nas/_rab tu byung nas 'jig
[\[102a.2\]]rten du de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas su 'gyur te/_sgra cher grags par 'gyur ro zhes bya ba'i bar du gsungs te/_dran pa dang ldan pa'i mchog dang /_blo gros dang ldan pa'i mchog dang /_bkur sti byed/_bla mar byed
[\[102a.3\]]ces bya ba nas rgyas par sbyar te/_'di ni de'i snga ltas yin no/_/'di la chos nyid ni 'di yin te/_de la 'di skad ces bya'o/_/gang tshe bde bar gshegs pa'i rje ngar ni/_/e ne ya'i 'dra gus pas chos 'dzin dang /_/'gro la phan phyir chos rnams ston pa dang /_/mang po rnams la
[\[102a.4\]]thugs brtse don mdzad dang /_/pha dang ma dang dge sbyong bram ze yi/_/phrin gyi bya ba slan chad mdzad gyur pa/_/las dge bde ba skyed par byed pa 'di/_/tshe rabs gzhan du ston pa de mdzad de/_/las kyi rnam par smin pa de nyid kyis/_/rje ngar e ne ya yi lta bur gyur/_/ci'i phyir byang chub
[\[102a.5\]]sems dpas skyes bu chen po'i mtshan shing n+ya gro d+ha lta bur chu zheng gab pa dang /_lus ma btud par lag pas pus mo'i lha ngar slebs pa gnyis thob ce na/_smras pa/_byang chub sems dpas ni sngon gyi srid pa zhes bya ba nas rgyas par sbyar te/_gnod par mi byed pa'i rang bzhin can du gyur
[\[102a.6\]]pas des su la yang lus dang ngag dang yid kyis gnod par ma byas pa dang /_gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' zas la tshod rig par gyur te/_ran par byed cing lto mi che ba dang /_lto 'dun mi byed cing lto 'dun gyi sbyor ba la mi brtson pa dang /_gzhan yang byang chub sems dpas ni 'di
[\[102a.7\]]lta ste/_zas dang /_skom dang /_bca' ba dang /_bza' ba dang /_gos dang /_spos dang /_me tog phreng dang /_byug pa dang /_mal cha dang /_stan dang /_gnas dang /_mar me'i sbyin pa rnams rang gi lag gis gus pa dang /_brnyas pa med par dus su sbyin pa dang /_gzhan yang byang
[\[102b\]]
[\[102b.1\]]chub sems dpas pha ma dang /_nye du dang /_rgan rabs dang /_bla ma lta bu rnams dang /_gzhan dge sbyong dang /_bram ze gnod par bya ba ma yin pa dang /_gnod par bya ba la mi dga' ba gang yin pa de dag na ba dang /_sdug cing phongs pa rnams dang /_nad tshabs che ba rnams la mthun pa'i sman
[\[102b.2\]]rnams dang /_phan pa'i zas rnams dang /_rkyen du 'tsham pa'i g.yog rnams byin te/_de las de dang /_yang dag par blangs pa de lta bu dang /_yang dag par bzung ba de lta bus lus zhig nas dga' ldan gyi lha rnams dang skal ba mnyam par skye'o zhes bya ba nas rgyas par sbyar te/_de de nas shi 'phos
[\[102b.3\]]nas khams 'dir mi rnams dang skal ba mnyam par skye'o zhes bya ba'i bar du rgyas par sbyar te/_der byang chub sems dpa' des skyes bu chen po'i mtshan shing n+ya gro d+ha ltar chu zhing gab pa dang /_lus ma btud par lag pas pus mo'i lha ngar slebs pa gnyis thob par 'gyur ro/_/de'i snga ltas
[\[102b.4\]]ni 'di yin te/_gal te khyim par 'dug cing khyim na gnas na ni 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po mtha' bzhir rgyal ba zhes bya ba nas rgyas par sbyar te/_gnod pa med cing nad med pa'i rang bzhin can dang /_bkur sti byed/_bla mar byed ces bya ba nas rgyas par sbyar ro/_/gal te skra dang kha spu
[\[102b.5\]]rnams bregs te/_gos ngur smrig dag bgos nas zhes bya ba nas rab tu byung na ni/_'jig rten du de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas su 'gyur te/_sgra cher grags par 'gyur ro zhes bya ba'i bar du gsungs te/_gnod pa med cing nad med pa'i rang
[\[102b.6\]]bzhin can dang /_bkur sti byed/_bla mar byed ces bya ba'i bar du rgyas par sbyar te/_'di ni de'i snga ltas yin no/_/'di la chos nyid ni 'di yin te/_de la 'di skad ces bya'o/_/chu zhing gab pa n+ya gro d+ha/_/ljon pa chen po sdong por ldan/_/yal ga lo ma phun sum tshogs/_/skyes bu mchog
[\[102b.7\]]ni de dang 'dra/_/lus ni thur du ma btud par/_/gyen du langs te 'dug bzhin du/_/pus mo'i lha nga gnyi ga yang /_/lag pa gnyis kyis kun du slebs/_/lus dang ngag dang de bzhin yid kyis kyang /_/'jig rten su la 'ang gnod pa yong mi byed/_/de bzhin mkhas pa zas la ran par byed/_/_
[\[103a\]]
[\[103a.1\]]des ni de dang de la tshod kyang rig_/gus par dus su brnyas pa med par ni/_/sngon gyi skye bar sbyin pa dag kyang byin/_/zas dang skom dang de bzhin gos rnams dang /_/spos dang me tog phreng dang byug pa dang /_/bdug pa phye ma de bzhin mal cha dang /_/bzhon pa de bzhin
[\[103a.2\]]gnas dang mar me dang /_/nad kyi gsos dang sman rnams pha ma dang /_/dge sbyong bram ze rnams la sngon byin te/_/las dge bde ba skyed par byed pa 'di/_/tshe rabs gzhan du ston pa des mdzad des/_/las kyi rnam par smin pa de yis ni/_/ston pa'i sku la mtshan ni 'di gnyis byung /_/ci'i phyir
[\[103a.3\]]byang chub sems dpas skyes bu chen po'i mtshan mdoms kyi spa ba sbubs su nub pa thob ce na/_smras pa/_byang chub sems dpas ni sngon gyi srid pa zhes bya ba nas rgyas par sbyar te/_pha ma dang /_nye du dang /_rgan rabs dang /_bla ma lta bu rnams dang /_gzhan dge sbyong dang /_bram ze gnod par bya
[\[103a.4\]]ba ma yin pa dang /_gnod par bya ba la mi dga' ba gang yin pa de dag grong dang /_zhing gang nas spyugs pa dang spangs pa de dag phyir chud par bya ba'i phyir shin tu spro ba drag po byas pa dang /_gzhan yang byang chub sems dpas ni bya ba dang /_don la gsol ba btab pa gang yin pa rnams dang /_phongs
[\[103a.5\]]pa byung ngo cog tu de dag bsgral ba dang /_kun du bsgral ba dang /_kun du rab tu bsgral ba'i phyir shin tu spro ba drag po byas te/_de gus par byed pa dang /_rtag tu byed pa dang /_gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' ngo tsha shes pa dang /_khrel yod par gyur pa dang /_gcer bu rnams 'gebs par byed pa yin
[\[103a.6\]]te/_de las de dang /_yang dag par blangs pa de lta bu dang /_yang dag par bzung ba de lta bus lus zhig nas dga' ldan gyi lha rnams dang skal ba mnyam par skye'o zhes bya ba nas rgyas par sbyar ro/_/de de nas shi 'phos nas khams 'dir mi rnams dang skal ba mnyam par skye'o zhes bya ba'i bar du rgyas
[\[103a.7\]]par sbyar te/_der byang chub sems dpa' des skyes bu chen po'i mtshan mdoms kyi sba ba sbubs su nub pa thob par 'gyur ro/_/de'i snga ltas ni 'di yin te/_gal te khyim par 'dug cing khyim na gnas na ni 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po mtha' bzhir rgyal ba zhes bya ba nas rgyas par sbyar te/_btsun
[\[103b\]]
[\[103b.1\]]mo'i 'khor dang /_gzhon nu rnams dang /_blon po rnams dang /_gtso bo dang /_dmag gi ru dang /_grong mi rnams dang /_yul gyi mi rnams kyis bsrung ba dang /_srung du bcug par 'gyur ba dang /_bkur sti byed/_bla mar byed ces bya ba nas rgyas par sbyar ro/_/gal te skra dang kha spu rnams
[\[103b.2\]]bregs te gos ngur smrig dag bgos nas zhes bya ba nas rab tu byung na ni 'jig rten du de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas su 'gyur te/_sgra cher grags par 'gyur ro zhes bya ba'i bar du gsungs te/_dge slong rnams dang /_dge slong ma rnams dang /_dge
[\[103b.3\]]bsnyen rnams dang /_dge bsnyen ma rnams kyis bsrung ba dang /_srung du bcug par 'gyur ba dang /_bkur sti byed/_bla mar byed ces bya ba'i bar du rgyas par sbyar te/_'di ni de'i snga ltas yin no/_/'di la chos nyid ni 'di yin te/_de la 'di skad ces bya'o/_/ci yi rgyus na mi mchog gi/_/mdoms
[\[103b.4\]]kyi sba ba sbubs su nub/_/spangs dang de yi thad du 'ongs/_/gang yin de ni sngon byas dang /_/gcer bu rnams ni bkab pa dang /_/ngo tsha shes dang khrel yod pa/_/des ni sbubs su nub par 'gyur/_/ci'i phyir byang chub sems dpas skyes bu chen po'i mtshan lus kyi pags pa srab pa dang /_spu re re nas
[\[103b.5\]]skye ba gnyis thob ce na/_smras pa/_byang chub sems dpa' ni sngon gyi srid pa zhes bya ba nas rgyas par sbyar te/_dge sbyong dang /_bram ze gsal ba dang /_yid gzhungs pa dang /_mkhas pa dang /_yongs su rdzogs par byed pa gang yin pa de dag gi thad du song nas bsten cing bsnyen te bsnyen bkur
[\[103b.6\]]byas nas/_dge ba'i las ni gang yin/_mi dge ba'i las ni gang yin/_kha na ma tho ba med pa dang /_kha na ma tho ba dang bcas pa ni gang yin/_gang byas na ni legs par 'gyur te/_sdig par mi 'gyur zhes dris shing dri ba'i bya ba byas te/_de dag las thos nas de dang de bzhin nyid du byas pa
[\[103b.7\]]dang /_gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' ni rtog par byed cing sems pa'i rang bzhin can du gyur pa dang /_gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' ni rtog par byed pa yin te/_pha ma dang /_nye du dang /_rgan rabs dang /_bla ma lta bu rnams dang /_gzhan dge sbyong dang /_bram ze gnod par
[\[104a\]]
[\[104a.1\]]bya ba ma yin pa dang /_gnod par bya ba la mi dga' ba gang yin pa de dag la dgab pa dang /_khrus bya ba dang /_mnye ba byas pa dang /_sa phyogs mi gtsang ba rnams gtsang bar byas te/_dag par byas shing phyag dar byas nas phyag dar rnams bor te/_de las de dang
[\[104a.2\]]yang dag par blangs pa de lta bu dang /_yang dag par bzung ba de lta bus lus zhig nas dga' ldan gyi lha rnams dang skal ba mnyam par skye'o zhes bya ba nas rgyas par sbyar ro/_/de de nas shi 'phos nas khams 'dir mi rnams dang skal ba mnyam par skye'o zhes bya ba'i bar du rgyas par sbyar te/_der
[\[104a.3\]]byang chub sems dpa' des skyes bu chen po'i mtshan lus kyi pags pa srab pa dang /_spu re re nas skye ba gnyis 'thob par 'gyur ro/_/de'i snga ltas ni 'di yin te/_gal te khyim par 'dug cing khyim na gnas na ni 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po mtha' bzhir rgyal ba zhes bya ba nas rgyas
[\[104a.4\]]par sbyar te/_dran pa dang ldan pa dang /_blo gros dang ldan par 'gyur zhing dran pa dang ldan pa'i mchog dang blo gros dang ldan pa'i mchog tu 'gyur ba dang /_bkur sti byed/_bla mar byed ces bya ba'i bar du sbyar ro/_/gal te skra dang kha spu rnams bregs te/_gos ngur smrig dag bgos
[\[104a.5\]]nas zhes bya ba nas/_rab tu byung na ni 'jig rten du de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas su 'gyur te/_sgra cher grags par 'gyur ro zhes bya ba'i bar du gsungs te/_dran pa dang ldan pa dang /_blo gros dang ldan par 'gyur zhing /_dran pa dang ldan
[\[104a.6\]]pa'i mchog dang /_blo gros dang ldan pa'i mchog tu 'gyur ba dang /_bkur sti byed/_bla mar byed ces bya ba'i bar du rgyas par sbyar te/_'di ni de'i snga ltas yin no/_/'di la chos nyid ni 'di yin te/_de la 'di skad ces bya'o/_/gang gis 'dir ni ston pa'i pags pa srab/_/gang tshe spu
[\[104a.7\]]rnams re rer skye bar 'gyur/_/mkhas brtags mang du thos pa bsten pa dang /_/rtogs par byed cing sems par gyur ba dang /_/sa phyogs rnams kyang gtsang mar byas pa dang /_/bsku zhing dril dang khrus rnams byas pa ste/_/las dge bde ba skyed par byed pa 'di/_/tshe rabs
[\[104b\]]
[\[104b.1\]]gzhan dag tu ni ston pas mdzad/_/las kyi rnam smin des na rgyal ba yi/_/pags pa srab cing spu rnams re rer skye/_/ci'i phyir byang chub sems dpas skyes bu chen po'i mtshan gser gyi kha dog dang /_'od 'dom gang ba gnyis thob ce na/_smras pa/_byang chub sems dpas ni sngon
[\[104b.2\]]gyi srid pa dang /_sngon gyi gnas dang /_sngon gyi lus dang /_sngon gyi bdag nyid thob pa dang /_sngon gyi tshe rabs gzhan dag dang /_'das pa dang /_zad pa dang /_'gags pa dang /_bral ba dang /_rnam par gyur pa dang /_yongs su zad pa dag tu pha ma dang /_nye du dang /_rgan rabs dang /_bla ma lta bu rnams
[\[104b.3\]]dang /_gzhan dge sbyong dang /_bram ze gnod par bya ba ma yin pa dang /_gnod par bya ba la mi dga' ba gang yin pa de dag la bca' ba dang bza' ba zhim po rnams byin pa dang /_khang khyim bzang po rnams dang /_gding ba dang /_bgo ba dang /_zas dang /_skom dang /_bca' ba dang /_
[\[104b.4\]]bza' ba dang /_gos dang /_spos dang /_byug pa dang /_mal cha dang /_stan dang /_gnas dang /_mar me bzang po rnams kyis sems kyi rgyud rnam par dag pas chos rnam par dag pa dang ldan pa'i sems can rnams la bya ba byas pa dang /_gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' khro ba med cing
[\[104b.5\]]khro gnyer dang bral bar 'gyur te/_de las de dang /_yang dag par blangs pa de lta bu dang /_yang dag par bzung ba de lta bus lus zhig nas dga' ldan gyi lha rnams dang skal ba mnyam par skye'o/_/de der skyes nas ring po ma lon par dga' ldan gyi ris kyi lha sngar skyes pa rnams las lha'i
[\[104b.6\]]gnas gsum gyis 'phags te/_gsum gang zhe na/_'di lta ste/_lha'i kha dog dang /_lha'i grags pas 'phags so/_/de der che'i tshad ji tsam pa de srid du gnas te/_de der tshe tshad ji tsam pa de srid du gnas nas de nas shi 'phos te khams 'dir mi rnams dang skal ba mnyam par skye'o/_/de

[\[105a\]]
[\[105a.1\]]'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po mtha' bzhir rgyal ba chos kyi rgyal po chos dang ldan pa/_rin po che sna bdun dang ldan par 'gyur ro/_/de'i rin po che sna bdun ni 'di lta bu yin te/_'di lta ste/_'khor lo rin po che nas/_bdun pa ste/_blon po rin po che'i bar

[\[105a.4\]]gces par byed/_bkur sti byed/_bla mar byed/_ri mor byed/_mchod par byed do/_/gal te skra dang kha spu rnams bregs te gos ngur smrig dag bgos nas/_dad pas khyim nas khyim med par legs pa kho nar rab tu byung na ni 'jig rten du de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par
[\[105a.5\]]rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas su 'gyur te/_sgra cher grags par 'gyur ro zhes gsungs te/_de gser gyi mdog de dang /_'od 'dom gang ba des dge slong rnams dang /_dge slong ma rnams dang /_dge bsnyen rnams dang /_dge bsnyen ma rnams dang /_lha rnams dang /_klu rnams dang /_lha ma
[\[105a.6\]]yin rnams dang /_nam mkha' lding rnams dang /_dri za rnams dang /_mi'am ci rnams dang /_lto 'phye chen po rnams dang /_gnod sbyin rnams dang /_srin po rnams dang /_mi rnams dang /_mi ma yin pa rnams kyis gces par byed/_bkur sti byed/_bla mar byed/_ri mor byed/_mchod

[\[105b.1\]]tshe rabs dag tu ston pa ni/_/khro ba med cing khro gnyer bral gyur te/_/las dge bde ba skyed pa byed pa 'di/_/tshe rabs gzhan dag tu ni ston pas mdzad/_/las kyi rnam par smin pa de yis na/_/gser gyi mdog can 'dom gang 'od dang ldan//_//rgyu gdags pa/_bam

[\[105b.3\]]ba rnams la sbyin pa mtho ba 'di lta ste/_zas dang /_skom dang /_bca' ba dang /_bza' ba dang /_gos dang /_spos dang /_me tog phreng dang /_byug pa dang /_mal cha dang /_stan dang /_gnas dang /_mar me dag byin te/_sems kyi rgyud rgya chen pos rnam par dag pa dang ldan pa'i

[\[106a\]]
[\[106a.1\]]dang /_bsam gtan dang /_rnam par thar pa dang /_ting nge 'dzin dang /_snyoms par 'jug pa dang /_yid la byed pa'i khyad par mtho bar 'gyur ba dang /_bkur sti byed/_bla mar byed ces bya ba'i bar du rgyas par sbyar te/_'di ni de'i snga ltas yin no/_/'di

[\[106b.1\]]khams 'dir mi rnams dang skal ba mnyam par skye'o zhes bya ba'i bar du rgyas par sbyar te/_der byang chub sems dpa' des skyes bu chen po'i mtshan ro stod seng ge'i 'dra ba dang /_thal gong rgyas pa dang /_dpung mgo shin tu zlum pa gsum thob par 'gyur ro/_/de'i snga ltas ni 'di yin te/_

[\[106b.5\]]bar gyur/_/sngon ni thal gong shin tu rgyas gyur dang /_/dpung mgo yang ni shin tu zlum par gyur/_/nan gyis mi 'dzin mchog tu 'dzin pa med/_/nyes par bsams pa legs spong brtul zhugs bzang /_/dge sbyong bram ze rnams kyis bzod par byed/_/des ni gnang bar bya ba'i chos rnams
[\[106b.6\]]gang /_/bde bar byed dang dge ba'i gtso bo gang /_/de dang de yang gtso bor bsko bar gyur/_/las dge bde ba skyed par byed pa 'di/_/tshe rabs gzhan dag tu ni ston pas mdzad/_/las kyi rnam smin des na ston pa yin/_/sku la mtshan ni 'di gsum byung bar gyur/_/ci'i phyir byang chub sems dpas

[\[107a\]]
[\[107a.1\]]rnams dbye ba'i phyir pha rol ba rnams la ma bsnyad la/_pha rol ba rnams kyi tshig thos na yang pha rol pa rnams dbye ba'i phyir tshu rol pa rnams kyi thad du 'ongs te ma bsnyad do/_/de ltar bye ba rnams gcig tu sdud pa dang /_'dus pa rnams la rjes su dga' ba dang mthun par

[\[107b\]]
[\[107b.1\]]dang /_/sngon ni rnam par smin dang mthun par byas/_/de ni 'dus pa rnams kyis de bzhin dga'/_/de bzhin du ni mgu zhing rangs par gyur/_/las dge bde bskyed par byed pa 'di/_/tshe rabs gzhan dag tu ni ston pas mdzad/_/las kyi rnam par smin pa de yis na/_/ston pa'i sku la mtshan

[\[108a\]]
[\[108a.1\]]byams pa thob/_/rtog par byed dang sems par gyur pa des/_/las dge bde ba skyed par byed pa 'di/_/tshe rabs gzhan dag tu ni ston pas mdzad/_/las kyi rnam par smin pa de yis na/_/bcom ldan mche ba shin tu dkar bar gyur/_/ci'i phyir byang chub

[\[108a.3\]]ma byin gyi bar du phyir gtang bar mi bya'o snyam ste/_de las de dang /_yang dag par blangs pa de lta bu dang /_yang dag par bzung ba de lta bus lus zhig nas dga' ldan gyi lha rnams dang skal ba mnyam par skye'o zhes bya ba nas rgyas par sbyar ro/_/de de nas shi 'phos nas khams 'dir mi rnams
[\[108a.4\]]dang skal ba mnyam par skye'o zhes bya ba'i bar du rgyas par sbyar te/_der byang chub sems dpa' des skyes bu chen po'i mtshan 'gram pa seng ge'i 'dra ba thob par 'gyur ro/_/de'i snga ltas ni 'di yin te/_gal te khyim par 'dug cing khyim na gnas na ni 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po mtha'

[\[108a.7\]]ci sgrub pa de dag thams cad rdzogs par thob par gyur pa dang /_bkur sti byed/_bla mar byed ces bya ba'i bar du rgyas par sbyar te/_'di ni de'i snga ltas yin no/_/'di la chos nyid ni 'di yin te/_de la 'di skad ces bya'o/_/sngon gyi tshe rabs gzhan du ston pa yi/_/thugs kyis thugs
[\[108b\]]
[\[108b.1\]]dam bcas pa 'di yin te/_/bdag la su yang rung ba ci slong yang /_/de ni bdag gis ma byin mi btang snyam/_/de ltar brtul zhugs dam pa rnam pa gsum/_/mtshan rdzogs de yi dgongs par ldan pa yis/_/sngon gyi tshe rabs gzhan du blangs par gyur/_/las kyi rnam smin des
[\[108b.2\]]na drang srong che/_/rgyal ba'i 'gram pa seng ge'i 'dra bar gyur/_/ci'i phyir byang chub sems dpas skyes bu chen po'i mtshan ro bro ba'i mchog thob ce na/_smras pa/_byang chub sems dpas ni sngon gyi srid pa zhes bya ba nas rgyas par sbyar te/_tho 'tshams pa med pa'i rang bzhin can du gyur nas/_
[\[108b.3\]]des sems can su la yang lag pa'am/_bong ba'am/_dbyug pa'am/_mtshon cha'am/_bsnun par bya ba gang yang rung bas tho 'tshams pa ma byas pa dang /_gzhan yang byang chub sems dpas pha ma dang /_nye du dang /_rgan rabs dang /_bla ma lta bu rnams dang /_gzhan dge sbyong dang /_bram ze
[\[108b.4\]]gnod par bya ba ma yin pa dang /_gnod par bya ba la mi dga' ba gang yin pa de dag la mthun pa'i sman rnams dang /_phan pa'i zas rnams dang /_'tsham pa'i g.yog byin te/_de las de dang /_yang dag par blangs pa de lta bu dang /_yang dag par bzung ba de lta bus lus zhig nas dga' ldan gyi
[\[108b.5\]]lha rnams dang skal ba mnyam par skye'o zhes bya ba nas rgyas par sbyar ro/_/de de nas shi 'phos nas khams 'dir mi rnams dang skal ba mnyam par skye'o zhes bya ba'i bar du rgyas par sbyar te/_der byang chub sems dpa' des skyes bu chen po'i mtshan ro bro ba'i mchog thob par 'gyur ro/_/de'i snga
[\[108b.6\]]ltas ni 'di yin te/_gal te khyim par 'dug cing khyim na gnas na ni/_'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po mtha' bzhir rgyal ba zhes bya ba nas rgyas par sbyar te/_gnod pa chung zhing nad med pa'i rang bzhin can du 'gyur ba dang /_bkur sti byed/_bla mar byed ces bya ba'i bar du rgyas par sbyar
[\[108b.7\]]ro/_/gal te skra dang kha spu rnams bregs te/_gos ngur smrig dag bgos nas dad pas khyim nas khyim med par legs pa kho nar rab tu byung na ni 'jig rten du de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas su 'gyur te/_sgra cher grags par 'gyur ro zhes bya
[\[109a\]]
[\[109a.1\]]ba'i bar du gsungs te/_gnod pa chung zhing nad med pa'i rang bzhin can du 'gyur ba dang /_bkur sti byed/_bla mar byed ces bya ba'i bar du rgyas par sbyar te/_/'di ni de'i snga ltas yin no/_/'di la chos nyid ni 'di yin te/_de la 'di skad ces bya'o/_/_
[\[109a.2\]]de yi lus la ro rnams bro ba'i mchog_/sngon ni 'khor ba'i tshe na gang las gyur/_/lag pa'am yang na dbyug pa'am mtshon cha yis/_/sems can su la'ang gnod par ma byas la/_/pha ma dang ni dge sbyong bram ze rnams/_/sngon ni nad kyi gsos sman dag kyang byin/_/las dge
[\[109a.3\]]bde bskyed par byed pa 'di/_/tshe rabs gzhan dag tu ni ston pas mdzad/_/las kyi rnam par smin pa de yis na/_/bcom ldan ro rnams bro ba'i mchog dang ldan/_/ci'i phyir byang chub sems dpas skyes bu chen po'i mtshan lce ring zhing srab pa dang /_mgo gtsug tor dang ldan pa
[\[109a.4\]]gnyis thob ce na/_smras pa/_byang chub sems dpas ni sngon gyi srid pa zhes bya ba nas rgyas par sbyar te/_bdag nyid kyang srog gcod pa spangs shing srog gcod pa las phyir log la/_gzhan dag kyang srog gcod pa spong ba yang dag par 'dzin du bcug pa dang /_bdag nyid kyang ma byin
[\[109a.5\]]par len pa dang /_'dod pas log par g.yem pa dang /_brdzun du smra ba dang /_'bru'i chang dang /_bcos pa'i chang myos par 'gyur ba bag med pa'i gnas spong ba yang dag par 'dzin du 'jug par byed de/_de las de dang /_yang dag par blangs pa de lta bu dang /_yang dag par bzung ba de
[\[109a.6\]]lta bus lus zhig nas dga' ldan gyi lha rnams dang skal ba mnyam par skye'o zhes bya ba nas rgyas par sbyar ro/_/de de nas shi 'phos nas khams 'dir mi rnams dang skal ba mnyam par skye'o zhes bya ba'i bar du rgyas par sbyar te/_der byang chub sems dpa' des skyes bu chen po'i mtshan lce ring zhing
[\[109a.7\]]srab pa dang /_mgo gtsug tor dang ldan pa gnyis thob par 'gyur ro/_/de'i snga ltas ni 'di yin te/_gal te khyim par 'dug cing khyim na gnas na ni/_'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po mtha' bzhir rgyal ba zhes bya ba nas rgyas par sbyar te/_lce ring zhing srab pa dang /_mgo gtsug tor dang ldan pa
[\[109b\]]
[\[109b.1\]]des gces par byed/_bkur sti byed/_bla mar byed ces bya ba'i bar du rgyas par sbyar ro/_/gal te skra dang kha spu rnams bregs te gos ngur smrig dag bgos nas/_dad pas khyim nas khyim med par legs pa kho nar rab tu byung na ni 'jig rten du de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang
[\[109b.2\]]dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas su 'gyur te/_sgra cher grags par 'gyur ro zhes bya ba'i bar du gsungs te/_de lce ring zhing srab pa dang /_mgo gtsug tor dang ldan pa des gces par byed/_bkur sti byed/_bla mar byed ces bya ba'i bar du rgyas par sbyar te/_'di ni de'i snga ltas
[\[109b.3\]]yin no/_/'di la chos nyid ni 'di yin te/_de la 'di skad ces bya'o/_/gang tshe rgyal ba'i dbu ni gtsug tor ldan/_/ljags kyang ring zhing srab par gang las gyur/_/srog chags ma bsad ma byin ma blangs dang /_/'dod na log par ma spyod brdzun ma byas/_/chang btung ba yang rtag
[\[109b.4\]]tu spang byas nas/_/mang po gzhan rnams kyang ni de la btsud/_/las dge bde ba skyed par byed pa 'di/_/tshe rabs gzhan dag tu ni ston pas mdzad/_/las kyi rnam smin des na rgyal ba yi/_/ljags kyang ring zhing srab la gtsug tor ldan/_/ci'i phyir byang chub sems dpas skyes bu chen
[\[109b.5\]]po'i mtshan tshangs pa'i dbyangs thob ce na/_smras pa/_byang chub sems dpas ni sngon gyi srid pa zhes bya ba nas rgyas par sbyar te/_tshig rtsub po spangs nas tshig rtsub po las phyir ldog ste/_de zhe gcod pa'i tshig rtsub po dang /_gzhan gyis mi bzod pa dang /_gzhan tshig pa za bar 'gyur
[\[109b.6\]]ba dang /_skye bo mang po'i yid du mi 'thad pa dang /_skye bo mang po mi dga' ba dang /_skye bo mang po'i yid du mi 'ong ba dang /_mnyam par gzhag pa ma yin pa dang /_ting nge 'dzin du mi 'gyur ba gang yin pa de lta bu'i tshig rnams spangs nas/_tshig snyan pa dang /_rnar snyan pa dang /_yid la
[\[109b.7\]]'bab pa dang /_dga' bar byed pa dang /_pho brang 'khor gyi skad dang /_snyan cing 'jebs pa dang /_gsal ba dang /_brda phrad pa dang /_mnyan par 'os pa dang /_rten pa med pa dang /_mi mthun pa med pa dang /_skye bo mang po'i 'dod pa dang /_skye bo mang po'i yid du 'thad pa dang /_skye
[\[110a\]]
[\[110a.1\]]bo mang po dga' ba dang /_skye bo mang po'i yid du 'ong ba dang /_shin tu mnyam par gzhag pa dang /_ting nge 'dzin du 'gyur ba gang yin pa lta bu'i tshig rnams smra bar byed do/_/gzhan yang byang chub sems dpas tshig kyal pa spangs nas tshig kyal pa las
[\[110a.2\]]slar log ste/_de dus su smra ba dang /_bden par smra ba dang /_don yod par smra ba dang /_brtags te smra ba dang /_gtan tshigs dang bcas pa dang /_gdams ngag dang bcas pa dang /_rigs pa dang mnyam par gzhag pa dang /_chos dang ldan pa dang /_don dang ldan pa dang /_ma 'dres
[\[110a.3\]]pa'i tshig rjod par byed de/_de las de dang yang dag par blangs pa de lta bu dang /_yang dag par bzung ba de lta bus lus zhig nas dga' ldan gyi lha rnams dang skal ba mnyam par skye'o zhes bya ba nas rgyas par sbyar ro/_/de de nas shi 'phos nas khams 'dir mi rnams dang skal ba mnyam par skye'o zhes
[\[110a.4\]]bya ba'i bar du rgyas par sbyar te/_der byang chub sems dpa' des skyes bu chen po'i mtshan tshangs pa'i dbyangs thob par 'gyur ro/_/de'i snga ltas ni 'di yin te/_gal te khyim par 'dug cing khyim na gnas na ni 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po mtha' bzhir rgyal ba zhes bya ba nas rgyas par sbyar
[\[110a.5\]]te/_de tshangs pa'i dbyangs des gces par byed/_bkur sti byed/_bla mar byed ces bya ba'i bar du rgyas par sbyar ro/_/gal te skra dang kha spu rnams bregs te gos ngur smrig dag bgos nas/_dad pas khyim nas khyim med par legs pa kho nar rab tu byung na ni 'jig rten du de bzhin
[\[110a.6\]]gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas su 'gyur te/_sgra cher grags par 'gyur ro zhes bya ba'i bar du gsungs te/_de tshangs pa'i dbyangs des gces par byed/_bkur sti byed/_bla mar byed ces bya ba'i bar du rgyas par sbyar te/_'di ni de'i snga ltas yin
[\[110a.7\]]no/_/'di la chos nyid ni 'di yin te/_de la 'di skad ces bya'o/_/tshangs pa'i dbyangs ni rnga sgra'i gdangs kyis mtshan/_/gang gis 'thob par 'gyur ba mnyan par gyis/_/'jam por smra zhing rtsub pa rnam par spangs/_/dga' ba smra zhing mi dga' smra mi byed/_/kyal pa'i tshig
[\[110b\]]
[\[110b.1\]]ni spangs par gyur pa dang /_/dus su don dang chos ni smra bar byed/_/las dge bde ba skyed par byed pa 'di/_/tshe rabs gzhan dag tu ni ston pas mdzad/_/las kyi rnam smin des na bde bar gshegs/_/drang srong chen po'i tshangs pa'i gsung dang ldan/_/ci'i phyir byang chub sems dpas
[\[110b.2\]]skyes bu chen po'i mtshan mig mthon mthing lta bu dang /_ba'i rdzi ma lta bu gnyis thob ce na/_smras pa/_byang chub sems dpas ni sngon gyi srid pa zhes bya ba nas rgyas par sbyar te/_'dod pa na spyod pa'i byams pa thob la/_de ni sems can du 'gyur bar 'dod pa gang yin pa rnams dang /_
[\[110b.3\]]don med par 'gyur bar 'dod pa gang yin pa rnams dang /_phan par 'dod pa gang yin pa rnams dang /_gnod par 'dod pa gang yin pa rnams dang /_bde bar 'dod pa gang yin pa rnams dang /_mi bde bar 'dod pa gang yin pa rnams dang /_bde ba la reg par 'dod pa gang yin pa rnams dang /_
[\[110b.4\]]bde ba la reg par mi 'dod pa gang yin pa rnams dang /_grub pa dang bde bar 'dod pa gang yin pa rnams dang /_grub pa dang bde bar mi 'dod pa gang yin pa de dag thams cad la byams pa'i mig gis bltas te/_dper na mas bu gcig pa sdug pa dang /_phangs pa dang /_dga' ba dang /_
[\[110b.5\]]yid du 'ong ba dang /_bzod cing mthong na mi mthun pa med de/_zla ba brgyad dam/_dgu lon gyi bar du ma phrad pa las mthong bar gyur na byams pa'i mig gis lta ba de bzhin du/_byang chub sems dpas kyang sems can don du 'gyur bar 'dod pa gang yin pa nas grub pa dang bde bar 'dod pa
[\[110b.6\]]gang yin pa'i bar gyi sems can de dag la byams pa'i mig gis bltas te/_de las de dang /_yang dag par blangs pa de lta bu dang /_yang dag par bzung ba de lta bus lus zhig nas dga' ldan gyi lha rnams dang skal ba mnyam par skye'o zhes bya ba nas rgyas par sbyar ro/_/de de nas shi

[\[111a\]]
[\[111a.1\]]'dug cing khyim na gnas na ni 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po mtha' bzhir rgyal ba zhes bya ba nas rgyas par sbyar te/_de mig mthon mthing lta bu dang /_ba'i rdzi ma lta bu des gces par byed/_bkur sti byed/_bla mar byed ces bya ba'i bar du rgyas par
[\[111a.2\]]sbyar ro/_/gal te skra dang kha spu rnams bregs te/_gos ngur smrig dag bgos nas dad pas khyim nas khyim med par legs pa kho nar rab tu byung na ni 'jig rten du de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas su 'gyur te/_sgra cher grags par 'gyur ro zhes
[\[111a.3\]]bya ba'i bar du gsungs te/_de mig mthon mthing lta bu dang /_ba'i rdzi ma lta bu des gces par byed/_bkur sti byed/_bla mar byed ces bya ba'i bar du rgya par sbyar te/_'di ni de'i snga ltas yin no/_/'di la chos nyid ni 'di yin te/_de la 'di skad ces bya'o/_/gang tshe bde
[\[111a.4\]]gshegs spyan ni mthon mthing ldan/_/gang tshe ston pa ba yi rdzi mar ldan/_/don 'dod gang yin don med 'dod pa gang /_/mi rnams bde reg mi 'dod gnod 'dod gang /_/ji ltar ma ni bu la snying brtse ba/_/de ltar thub pas 'jig rten kun la gzigs/_/las dge bde ba skyed par
[\[111a.5\]]byed pa 'di/_/tshe rabs gzhan dag tu ni ston pas mdzad/_/las kyi rnam smin des kyin ston pa yi/_/sku la mtshan ni rnam gnyis byung bar gyur/_/ci'i phyir byang chub sems dpas skyes bu chen po'i mtshan smin mtshams kyi mdzod spu thob ce na/_smras pa/_byang chub sems dpas ni sngon
[\[111a.6\]]gyi srid pa dang /_sngon gyi gnas dang /_sngon gyi lus dang /_sngon gyi bdag nyid thob pa dang /_sngon gyi tshe rabs gzhan dag dang /_'das pa dang /_zad pa dang /_'gags pa dang /_bral ba dang /_rnam par gyur pa dang /_yongs su zad pa dag tu pha ma dang /_nye du dang /_rgan rabs dang /_
[\[111a.7\]]bla ma lta bu rnams dang /_gzhan dge sbyong dang /_bram ze gnod par bya ba ma yin pa dang /_gnod par bya ba la mi dga' ba gang yin pa de dag gis bsngags pa dus su bden par bsgrags te/_de las de dang /_yang dag par blangs pa de lta bu dang /_yang dag par bzung ba de lta bus lus
[\[111b\]]
[\[111b.1\]]zhig nas dga' ldan gyi lha rnams dang skal ba mnyam par skye'o/_/de der skyes nas ring po ma lon par dga' ldan gyi ris kyi lha sngar skyes pa rnams las lha'i gnas gsum gyis 'phags te/_gsum gang zhe na/_'di lta ste/_lha'i tshe dang /_lha'i kha dog dang /_lha'i grags
[\[111b.2\]]pas 'phags so/_/de der tshe'i tshad ji tsam pa de srid du gnas nas/_de nas shi 'phos te khams 'dir mi rnams dang skal ba mnyam par skye'o/_/de 'dir rgyal po'i pho brang ngam/_mdun na 'don gyi khyim du skye bar 'gyur te/_der byang chub sems dpa' des skyes bu chen
[\[111b.3\]]po'i mtshan smin mtshams kyi mdzod spu thob par 'gyur ro/_/de'i snga ltas ni 'di yin te/_gal te khyim par 'dug cing khyim na gnas na ni 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po mtha' bzhir rgyal ba chos kyi rgyal po chos dang ldan pa rin po che sna bdun dang ldan par 'gyur ro/_/de'i rin po che
[\[111b.4\]]sna bdun ni 'di dag yin te/_'di lta ste/_'khor lo rin po che dang /_glang po rin po che dang /_rta rin po che dang /_nor bu rin po che dang /_bud med rin po che dang /_khyim bdag rin po che dang /_bdun pa ste/_blon po rin po che'o/_/de'i bu ni stong tham pa yod dpa' ba rtul phod pa/_
[\[111b.5\]]yan lag mchog gi gzugs dang ldan pa pha rol gyi sde rab tu 'joms pa sha stag go/_/de'i rgya mtsho la thug pa'i sa chen po ma lus pa gnod par sngo ba med cing 'tshe ba med pa 'di nyid chad pa med cing mtshon gyis bda' ba med la/_chos dang mthun zhing snyoms pas legs par phab ste gnas
[\[111b.6\]]la/_gang gi tshe 'jig rten du 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po byung bar gyur pa na sgra de skye bo mang po'i dga' ba yid du 'ong bar 'gyur te/_sgra de yang gzhan 'phrul dbang byed kyi lha rnams kyi bar du grags par 'gyur te/_btsun mo'i 'khor dang /_gzhon nu rnams dang /_blon po rnams dang /_
[\[111b.7\]]gtso bo dang /_dmag gi ru dang /_grong mi dang /_yul gyi mi rnams kyis bkur sti byed/_bla mar byed/_ri mor byed/_mchod pa byed do/_/gal te skra dang kha spu rnams bregs te/_gos ngur smrig dag bgos nas/_dad pas khyim nas khyim med par legs pa kho nar rab tu byung na ni/_

[\[112a.1\]]'jig rten du de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas su 'gyur te/_sgra cher grags par 'gyur ro zhes gsungs te/_gang gi tshe 'jig rten du de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs

[\[112a.6\]]gdags pa'i bstan bcos rgyu gdags pa las/_/mtshan gyi phung po zhes bya ba phung po dang po rdzogs so//_//gleng gzhi ni mnyan du yod pa na ste/_dge slong dag 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po 'jig rten du byung na rin po che sna bdun 'jig rten du 'byung bar 'gyur te/_bdun
[\[112a.7\]]gang zhe na/_'di lta ste/_'khor lo rin po che dang /_glang po rin po che dang /_rta rin po che dang /_nor bu rin po che dang /_bud med rin po che dang /_khyim bdag rin po che dang /_bdun pa ste/_blon po rin po che'o/_/dge slong dag de ltar na 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po 'jig rten du byung
[\[112b\]]
[\[112b.1\]]na rin po che sna bdun de lta bu dag 'jig rten du 'byung bar 'gyur ro/_/dge slong dag de bzhin du de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas 'jig rten du byung na byang chub kyi yan lag rin po che bdun 'jig rten du 'byung bar 'gyur te/_bdun gang zhe na/_

[\[112b.3\]]de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas 'jig rten du byung na byang chub kyi yan lag rin po che bdun po de lta bu dag 'jig rten du 'byung bar 'gyur ro zhes de skad gsungs so/_/ci'i phyir 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal pos 'khor lo rin po che thob par 'gyur
[\[112b.4\]]zhe na/_smras pa/_'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal pos ni sngon gyi srid pa zhes bya ba nas rgyas par sbyar te/_bdag nyid kyis kyang srog gcod pa spangs shing srog gcod pa las phyir log ste/_dbyug pa spangs shing mtshon cha spangs la ngo tsha shes shing snying rje dang ldan te/_srog chags
[\[112b.5\]]su gyur pa'i sems can thams cad las tha na srog chags grogs sbur yan chad kyi srog gcod pa las sems yongs su sbyangs la/_gzhan dag kyang srog gcod pa spong ba yang dag par 'dzin du bcug pa dang /_bdag nyid kyis kyang ma byin par len pa dang /_'dod pa la log par
[\[112b.6\]]g.yem pa dang /_brdzun du smra ba dang /_phra ma dang /_tshig rtsub po dang /_tshig kyal pa dang /_brnab sems dang /_gnod sems dang /_log par lta ba spangs nas yang dag pa'i lta ba can du gyur la/_gzhan dag kyang yang dag pa'i lta ba yang dag par 'dzin du bcug pas na/_de
[\[112b.7\]]gso sbyong gi dus tshes bco lnga de nyid kyi tshe khrus byas nas gso sbyong blangs te blon po'i tshogs kyis bskor ba na/_nyi ma 'char ka'i tshe shar phyogs nas lha'i 'khor lo rin po che rtsibs stong ba lte ba dang bcas mu khyud dang bcas pa dag cing gtsang la mkhan bzos ma byas pa lha rdzas ril
[\[113a\]]
[\[113a.1\]]gyis gser las grub pa 'byung bar 'gyur te/_der rgyal rigs spyi bo nas dbang bskur ba'i rgyal pos mthong nas de 'di snyam du sems te/_bdag gis sngon gyi 'khor los sgyur ba rnams kyi gtam thos na/_rgyal rigs spyi bo nas dbang bskur ba'i rgyal po
[\[113a.2\]]gang la gso sbyong gi tshul tshes bco lnga de nyid kyi tshe khrus byas nas gso sbyong blangs te/_blon po'i tshogs kyis bskor ba na/_nyi ma 'char ka'i tshe shar phyogs nas lha'i 'khor lo rin po che rtsibs stong pa lte ba dang bcas mu khyud dang bcas pa dag cing gtsang la mkhan bzos ma byas pa lha
[\[113a.3\]]rdzas ril gyis gser las grub pa 'byung bar 'gyur ba de'i 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal por 'gyur ro zhes zer ba dang sbyar na/_bdag ni 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po yin par nges so snyam mo/_/de nas 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po stan las langs te bla gos phrag pa gcig tu
[\[113a.4\]]gzar nas bus mo g.yas pa'i lha nga sa la btsugs te/_lha'i 'khor lo rin po che lag pa gnyis kyis blangs nas lag pa g.yon par bzhag ste/_lag pa g.yas pas shar phyogs logs su phul nas 'di skad du/_'khor lo rin po che sngon gyi 'phags pa 'khor los sgyur ba'i
[\[113a.5\]]lam gang yin pa las rnam par rgyal bar gyis shig_/kye 'khor lo rin po che sngon gyi 'phags pa 'khor los sgyur ba'i lam gang yin pa las rnam par rgyal bar gyis shig_/rnam par rgyal bar gyis shig ces byas nas lha'i 'khor lo rin po che sngon gyi 'khor los sgyur ba'i lam
[\[113a.6\]]gang yin par 'gro bar 'gyur ro/_/'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po yang dpung gi tshogs yan lag bzhi pa dang lhan cig tu lha'i 'khor lo rin po che de'i phyi bzhin 'gro bar 'gyur la/_lha'i 'khor lo rin po che phyogs gang du sdod pa der 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po dpung gi tshogs yan
[\[113a.7\]]lag bzhi pa dang lhan cig tu mtshan mo'i dgongs mal 'debs so/_/shar phyogs kyi rgyal phran ji snyed yod pa de dag thams cad 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po ga la ba der dong ste lhags nas 'di skad du/_lha tshur gshegs lha gshegs pa legs so/_/yul 'di dag ni lha'i
[\[113b\]]
[\[113b.1\]]lags te/_'byor pa dang /_rgyas pa dang /_bde ba dang /_lo legs pa dang /_skye bo dang mi mang pos gang ba lags kyi/_'di dag lhas legs par gdul du gsol/_bdag cag ni lha'i zham ring 'tshal lo zhes zer to/_/'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal pos kyang de dag la
[\[113b.2\]]'di skad du/_yul gyi gtso bo dag de bas na rang rang gi yul 'khor ji lta ba bzhin du chos dang mthun par legs par thul cig_/chos ma yin pas ma byed cig_/yul 'khor 'dir chos ma yin pa spyod pa dang /_'gal bar byed pa su yang gnas su ma gzhag cig_/de ltar byed
[\[113b.3\]]dang khyed nga'i zham ring byed pa yin no zhes bsgo'o/_/de nas lha'i 'khor lo rin po ches shar phyogs legs par btul te shar phyogs kyi rgya mtsho chen po las brgal nas lho phyogs su sngon gyi 'phags pa 'khor los sgyur ba'i lam gang yin pa logs su 'gro ste/_'khor los
[\[113b.4\]]sgyur ba'i lam der 'khor lo rin po che 'gro'o/_/'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po yang dpung gi tshogs yan lag bzhi pa dang lhan cig tu lha'i 'khor lo rin po che de'i phyi bzhin 'gro bar 'gyur la/_lha'i 'khor lo rin po che phyogs gang du sdod pa der 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po dpung gi
[\[113b.5\]]tshogs yan lag bzhi pa dang lhan cig tu mtshan mo'i dgongs mal 'debs so/_/lho phyogs kyi rgyal phran ji snyed yod pa de dag thams cad kyang 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po ga la ba der dong ste zhes bya ba nas rgyas par sngar ji skad bstan pa bzhin du brjod par bya'o/_/de nas lha'i
[\[113b.6\]]'khor lo rin po ches lho phyogs legs par btul te lho phyogs kyi rgya mtsho las brgal nas nub phyogs su sngon gyi 'phags pa 'khor los sgyur ba'i lam gang yin pa logs su 'gro ste/_'khor los sgyur ba'i lam der lha'i 'khor lo rin po che 'gro'o/_/'khor los sgyur ba'i
[\[113b.7\]]rgyal po yang dpung gi tshogs yan lag bzhi pa dang lhan cig tu lha'i 'khor lo rin po che de'i phyi bzhin du 'gro bar 'gyur la/_lha'i 'khor lo rin po che phyogs gang du sdod pa der 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po dpung gi tshogs yan lag bzhi pa dang lhan cig tu mtshan mo'i dgongs mal 'debs
[\[114a\]]

[\[114b\]]
[\[114b.1\]]sgyur ba'i rgyal po yang yod do/_/gang gi zangs kyi 'khor lo 'byung bar 'gyur ba'i 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po yang yod do/_/gang gi lcags kyi 'khor lo 'byung bar 'gyur ba'i 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po yang yod do/_/de las 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po gang gi

[\[117a.3\]]bzhi pa glang po che'i tshogs dang /_rta pa'i tshogs dang /_shing rta'i tshogs dang /_dpung bu chung gi tshogs go cha bgos nas 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal bo dang /_g.yul 'gyed pa'i phyir 'byung bar byed de/_'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po dang 'thab pa dang /_mtshang

[\[117b\]]
[\[117b.1\]]phyogs nas lha'i 'khor lo rin po che rtsibs stong pa lte ba dang bcas mu khyud dang bcas pa dag cing gtsang la mkhan bzos ma byas pa/_lha rdzas ril gyis lcags las grub pa 'byung bar 'gyur te/_der rgyal rigs spyi bo nas dbang bskur ba'i rgyal pos mthong nas de 'di snyam du

[\[117b.3\]]tshe shar phyogs nas lha'i 'khor lo rin po che rtsibs stong pa/_lte ba dang bcas pa dag cing gtsang la mkhan bzos ma byas pa/_lha rdzas ril gyis lcags las grub pa 'byung bar 'gyur ba de/_'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal por 'gyur ro zhes zer ba dang sbyar na/_bdag ni 'khor
[\[117b.4\]]los sgyur ba'i rgyal po yin par nges so snyam mo/_/de nas 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po stan las langs te/_bla gos phrag pa gcig tu gzar nas pus mo g.yas pa'i lha nga sa la btsugs te/_lha'i 'khor lo rin po che lag pa gnyis kyis blangs nas lag pa g.yon par
[\[117b.5\]]bzhag ste/_lag pa g.yas pas shar phyogs logs su phul nas/_'di skad du 'khor lo rin po che sngon gyi 'phags pa 'khor los sgyur ba'i lam gang yin pa las rnam par rgyal bar gyis shig_/kye 'khor lo rin po che sngon gyi 'phags pa 'khor los sgyur ba'i lam
[\[117b.6\]]gang yin pa las rnam par rgyal bar gyis shig_/rnam par rgyal bar gyis shig ces bya ba na/_lha'i 'khor lo rin po che sngon gyi 'khor los sgyur ba'i lam gang yin par 'gro bar 'gyur ro/_/'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po yang dpung gi tshogs yan lag bzhi pa dang lhan
[\[117b.7\]]cig tu lha'i 'khor lo rin po che de'i phyi bzhin 'gro bar 'gyur la lha'i 'khor lo rin po che phyogs gang du sdod pa der 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po dpung gi tshogs yan lag bzhi pa dang lhan cig tu mtshan mo'i dgongs mal 'debs so/_/shar phyogs kyi rgyal phran rnams

[\[118a.1\]]/kyis kyang /_'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po gshegs so zhes thos so/_/thos nas kyang dpung gi tshogs yan lag bzhi pa glang bo che'i tshogs dang /_rta'i tshogs dang /_shing rta'i tshogs dang /_dpung bu chung gi tshogs go cha bskor nas/_
[\[118a.2\]]'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po dang g.yul 'gyed pa'i phyir 'byung bar byed de/_'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po dang 'thab pa dang /_mtshang 'dru ba dang /_'gyed pa dang /_rtsod par byed cing /_mtshon bzo bar byed kyi/_gcig la gcig gsod par ni mi byed kyi/_de dag dang 'thab

[\[118a.7\]]po 'khor los sgyur ba yis/_/de dag la ni 'di skad bsgo/_/yul gyi gtso rnams de bas na/_/rang rang gi ni yul 'khor rnams/_/chos bzhin du ni gdul bar gyis/_/chos min spyod dang mi mthun spyod/_/su yang 'dir ni gnas ma gzhug_/de ltar byed na khyed rnams kyang /_/nga yi

[\[118b.1\]]zham ring byed pa yin/_/gang la mi ma yin pa yi/_/dngul gyi 'khor lo 'byung 'gyur ba/_/des ni tshul khrims yang dag blangs/_/des na snga nas dman pa med/_/rgyal po de ni rdzu 'phrul che/_/sa steng 'di ni thul bar 'gyur/_/de la rgyal phran rnams kyis ni/_/bsu zhing smra bar
[\[118b.2\]]mi byed de/_/'ongs nas der ni 'gro ba dang /_/myur du de dang mthun par byed/_/tshur gshegs lha ni gshegs pa legs/_/yul ni 'di dag khyod kyi lags/_/'di dag lha yis gdul du gsol/_/bdag cag khyod kyi zham ring 'tshal/_/rgyal po chos dang ldan pa yis/_/_

[\[119a.1\]]lo rin po che rtsibs stong pa lte ba dang bcas mu khyud dang bcas pa/_rnam pa thams cad yongs su rdzogs pa dag pa bzang ba/_mkhan bzos ma byas pa/_lha rdzas ril gyis gser las grub pa mngon par sprul to/_/de nas lha'i bu las thams cad pas/_

[\[120a\]]
[\[120a.1\]]pa 'di bskor te/_rgyal po'i pho brang de nyid du 'ongs nas khye'u sus za'o/_/'di la chos nyid ni 'di yin te/_de la 'di skad ces bya'o/_/bde ba'i bzhon pa byin pa dang /_/bzhon ba mang po byin pa dang /_/glang po rin chen mang dang khyogs/_/smyig 'khar sba

[\[121a.1\]]'tshal zhes byas nas/_'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal pos bsgo ba bzhin du mnyan te/_rta rin po che'i brda rnams slob du bcug nas/_nyi ma gcig gis brda thams cad lobs te/_dper na de ma yin pa'i rta rnams lo du ma lo brgya phrag du mas

[\[121a.6\]]rgyal po sprin gyi shugs can zhes bya ba gzugs bzang zhing blta na sdug la mdzes pa/_thams cad sngo la mgo bo gnag cing phum phum yid du 'ong ba zhig gnas so/_/de'i 'khor rta'i rgyal po khri brgyad stong yod de/_de dag thams cad kyang gzugs bzang zhing blta na sdug la

[\[121b.1\]]sgyur ba'i rgyal po 'jig rten du byung ba shes par gyis la de'i rta rin po che thang shig_/de nas rta'i rgyal po sprin gyi shugs can gyis lha rnams kyi dbang po brgya byin gyis bsgo ba bzhin du/_mnyan nas bu thu bo gtong bar byed de/_gal te de ches sngar 'chi bar gyur na ni de'i tshe des yang de'i 'og

[\[121b.4\]]mar me'i snying po dang /_mar me'i snod rnams byin pa dang /_sgron ma rnams dang /_mar me rnams dang /_snang ba rnams byas nas mun pa chen po med par byas te/_de bas na 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal pos nor bu rin po che thob bo/_/nor bu rin po che de yang bai DUR+Ya zur brgyad pa/_bzang po
[\[121b.5\]]rags pa che ba/_dag cing rnyog pa med pa/_rnam par gsal ba ste/_'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po'i btsun mo'i 'khor du snang ba ci tsam dgos pa thams cad nor bu de'i 'od kyis byed do/_/de nas 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal pos/_nor bu rin po che de sad par 'dod de/_de nas

[\[122a\]]
[\[122a.1\]]rnams/_/lhug par gtong dang ldan pas byin/_/gzhan yang snang dang gsal ba dang /_/sgron ma 'bar ba rnams kyang byin/_/de nas rgyal pos gsal dag pa'i/_/bai DUR+Ya yi nor bu thob/_/nor bu rin po che de ga las 'ongs she na/_smras pa/_gang
[\[122a.2\]]gi tshe 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po 'jig rten du 'byung ba na/_de la klu rnams sam/_yang na rgyal po chen po bzhis 'bul bar byed do/_/ci'i phyir 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal pos bud med rin po che thob ce na/_smras pa/_'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal pos ni/_sngon gyi srid pa zhes bya ba
[\[122a.3\]]nas rgyas par sbyar te/_dge sbyong dang /_bram ze rnams dang /_bkren pa rnams dang /_sdug phongs pa rnams la sbyin pa 'di lta ste/_zas dang /_skam dang /_bca' ba dang /_bza' ba dang /_gos dang /_spos dang /_me tog phreng dang /_byug pa dang /_mal cha dang /_stan dang /_

[\[122a.5\]]yang mi sngo ste/_pags pa'i mdog pri yang ku'i me tog ltar 'dug la/_ha cang yang mi ring /_ha cang yang mi thung ste/_lus ran par 'dug pa dang /_ha cang skem pa yang ma yin ha cang sha che ba yang ma yin te/_sha ran la btsun mo de grang ba'i dus na ni lus rnams la reg na dro bar 'gyur

[\[122b\]]

[\[123a.1\]]tshogs pa dang /_ro phun sum tshogs pa rnams rang gi lag nas gus par byas te/_ma brnyas par dus su byin te/_rgyu des na bud med rin po che ha cang yang mi dkar/_ha cang yang mi sngo ste/_pags pa'i mdog pri yang ku'i me tog ltar 'dug la/_ha

[\[124a.1\]]che bar grags pa'i sems can yin pas na/_de'i phyir de sems dman pa'i mi la sems 'jug par mi 'gyur te/_rgyu des na bud med rin po che yid kyi dgu la yang 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po'i yid dang 'gal bar mi byed na lus dang /_ngag gis

[\[195a.1\]]'am/_lag rtsis sam/_bzo'i gnas sam/_las kyi gnas gang yang rung ba'i sgo nas grong dang /_grong rdal dang /_yul 'khor dang /_rgyal po'i pho brang de dang de dag tu bskos na/_des longs spyod de dag 'dod nas/_gzhan la tshig rtsub po kun du spyod

[\[229a.1\]]du mtshon cha dang /_me dang /_dug dang /_dbyug pas bsnun pa la sogs pa thabs rnam pa sna tshogs kyis bsad pa yang de dang 'dra bar brjod par bya'o/_/spun drung gis spun drung la ji lta ba bzhin du ming pos sring mo la bsgo ba dang /_sring mos ming po la bsgo ba dang /_

[\[229a.3\]]pa/_ldan par ni mi 'gyur ro/_/nye du ma yin pa'i bud med du 'du shes pas/_nye du ma yin pa'i bud med gsad par bya'o snyam pa las/_ma bsad par gyur na/_de ci mtshams med pa'i las dang ldan par 'gyur ram/_'on te ldan par mi 'gyur zhe na/_smras pa/_
[\[229a.4\]]ldan par mi 'gyur ro/_/nye du ma yin pa'i bud med yin par 'du shes pas/_nye du ma yin pa'i bud med bsad na/_de ci mtshams med pa'i las dang ldan par 'gyur ram/_'on te ldan par mi 'gyur zhe na/_smras pa/_gal te dgra bcom ma bsad par gyur na ni/_de

[\[229a.6\]]dang 'dra'o/_/spyi sdom ni/_ched du byas dang rtsa ba dang /_/rgyu med pa dang chung ngu dang /_/las dang yang dag ma bsdams pa/_/de yi gzhi dang sum cu drug_/'das pa'i rgyu las byung ba dang /_/rtsa bzad dang tshe zad pa'o/_/chos mngon pa las las gdags pa bshad pa
